# AIRA — 25 FULL REEL CONCEPTS (Complete Set)

> Built to full SYS.txt spec. Tools: **Nano Banana Pro** (stills) + **VEO 3.1** (video) only.
> Identity carried by reference image — text always uses `Aira, [placeholder]`, never describes her likeness.
> Vibrant/saturated color enforced. One motivated magic move per concept. Perfect loop. Sound is boss.
> Anti-flip: Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject in any frame.
> Subject framing: Every frame specifies exact body-portion, screen-position, and distance from camera.

---

# AIRA — NEW REEL CONCEPTS (Beyond GRWM / Beyond Beauty-Ad)

> Built to full SYS.txt spec. Tools: **Nano Banana Pro** (stills) + **VEO 3.1** (video) only.
> Identity carried by reference image — text always uses `Aira, [placeholder]`, never describes her likeness.
> Vibrant/saturated color enforced. One motivated magic move per concept. Perfect loop. Sound is boss.

---

## SPEC APPLIED TO EVERY CONCEPT (reference)

**Image prompt sections:** Subject (`Aira, [placeholder]`) · Hairstyle (unique per concept) · Wardrobe · Footwear · Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories (where suitable) · Pose & Framing (pose type + how much of body in frame) · Camera (angle + height + lens) · Background (powerful, striking) · Lighting (layered) · Color & Vibrance · Composition · Facial Expression (fluid, heavily detailed) · Object Interaction.

**Video prompt sections:** Camera Movement (continuous, timed) · Subject Action (timed) · Object Action (timed) · Physics (detailed) · Object Interaction (timed, perfect contact) · Facial Expression Beats (fluid, timed — eyes lead → mouth follows → blink → breath) · Lighting Behavior · Lens / Optical · Diegetic Sound (exact, timed) · Loop note.

**Pose & angle pool used across frames:** front · side/profile · three-quarter · back pose · over-the-shoulder · low angle · high angle · overhead/top-down · eye-level · Dutch tilt.
**Framing pool:** extreme close-up / macro · close-up · medium close-up · medium · medium-full · full body · wide.

**External AUDIO BLOCK** follows every concept — for the background music / sound bed laid under the cut.

---

# IDEA A — THE EVERYDAY-THING-GOES-MAGIC
*Feeling: delight / surprise. Aira treats the impossible as totally normal; the viewer is the only one amazed.*

## CONCEPT A-1 — "The Upside-Down Pour"

- **Feeling:** delight / quiet surprise
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** sleek ultra-glossy high ponytail, razor-sharp center part, a single face-framing strand left loose, baby-hairs laid
- **Magic move (the one impossible thing):** coffee pours **upward** — from the cup back into the carafe, against gravity — and Aira is completely unbothered
- **Concept line:** "mornings hit different"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move through a sunrise penthouse kitchen, 7 frames flowing as a single camera travel
- **Loop:** final frame returns the carafe to the exact start position so the pour can begin again seamlessly

---

### FRAME 1 — establishing | wide | full body | front pose | low-ish eye level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, standing relaxed at a marble kitchen island, weight on one hip, calm and self-possessed.
- **Hairstyle:** sleek ultra-glossy high ponytail, razor-sharp center part, one loose face-framing strand, laid baby-hairs.
- **Wardrobe:** a tailored oversized ivory silk shirt worn as a dress, sleeves pushed to the forearm, one shoulder slightly dropped; cinched with a thin gold chain belt.
- **Footwear:** barefoot on warm oak floor, toes relaxed, a single thin gold ankle chain.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** small gold hoop earrings, two stacked thin rings, glossy nude almond nails; a thin gold watch.
- **Pose & Framing:** full-body front pose, slight three-quarter turn of the torso toward the island; she occupies the right third, head-to-feet in frame.
- **Camera:** eye-level, very slight low tilt, 35mm full-frame look, deep enough focus to read the room.
- **Background (powerful):** a vast penthouse kitchen behind floor-to-ceiling glass overlooking a glowing sunrise skyline above a soft sea of low clouds; warm gold light flooding in, polished marble, brushed-brass fixtures, a single tall vibrant orange bird-of-paradise flower in a glass vase as the saturated color anchor.
- **Lighting:** key = warm low sunrise sun through glass (camera-left, raking); fill = soft bounce off white marble; rim = bright sun edge on her ponytail and shoulder; practical = under-cabinet warm strip.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated golden-amber sunrise + the vivid orange flower + cool blue cloud-sea outside for contrast; rich blacks, glossy highlights, no washed-out tones.
- **Composition:** glass and skyline fill the left two-thirds, Aira anchors right, the carafe and cup sit on the island in the lower-center as the future action point.
- **Facial Expression:** serene, lids relaxed at about three-quarter open, a faint knowing smile resting only in the corners of the mouth, brow smooth and slightly lifted — completely at ease.
- **Object Interaction:** fingertips of her right hand rest lightly on the cool marble, the other hand loose at her side.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:03 slow push-in from the wide, drifting from low eye-level toward the island, easing as it settles.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:02 she breathes in slowly (chest lifts), weight shifts subtly hip-to-hip; 0:02–0:03 her gaze slides down to the cup.
- **Object Action:** carafe and cup sit still; steam rises off the cup in slow lazy curls drifting camera-left with the airflow.
- **Physics:** silk shirt hem sways with a soft delayed weight as she shifts; ponytail has natural pendulum settle; steam obeys slow convection, thinning as it rises; ankle chain micro-swings.
- **Object Interaction:** her fingertips maintain believable soft contact with marble — slight skin flatten at the contact point, no floating.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00–0:01 calm neutral, slow blink; 0:01–0:02 eyes drift down (eyes lead), corner-smile deepens a touch; 0:02–0:03 a soft settle, gentle exhale.
- **Lighting Behavior:** sun ray strength pulses up almost imperceptibly as a thin cloud clears outside, lifting the rim light on her hair.
- **Lens / Optical:** gentle focus settle from deep to a touch shallower as the push-in lands, background skyline softening slightly.
- **Diegetic Sound:** distant muffled city hum below; soft room tone; a faint ceramic settle; the low fizz/curl of steam; one slow breath; a quiet morning bird far outside the glass.
- **Loop note:** carafe/cup positions are the master reference for the final frame.

---

### FRAME 2 — over-the-shoulder | medium-full | back/over-shoulder pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, seen from behind over her right shoulder as she steps to the island and reaches for the carafe.
- **Hairstyle:** same glossy high ponytail — now we read its full length and razor part from behind, individual glossy strands catching rim light.
- **Wardrobe:** ivory silk shirt-dress from the back, soft drape across the shoulder blades, gold chain belt knot visible.
- **Footwear:** barefoot, one heel lifting as she steps.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** gold hoop catches light at the jaw; rings visible on the reaching hand.
- **Pose & Framing:** back pose / over-the-shoulder, medium-full (mid-thigh up), her shoulder and ponytail frame the left edge, the carafe and cup in the focal pocket beyond her hand.
- **Camera:** eye-level behind her, lens looking past her shoulder, 50mm; she is soft-foreground, the carafe is the sharp subject.
- **Background (powerful):** the glowing skyline and cloud-sea now fill the deep background through the glass, blazing warm; the vibrant orange flower sits sharp mid-frame.
- **Lighting:** strong sun rim down her back and ponytail; soft frontal bounce on the carafe; warm glow halo around her silhouette.
- **Color & Vibrance:** intense backlit gold halo, deep saturated shadows on her front-facing-away side, the orange flower popping.
- **Composition:** classic OTS — her shoulder anchors lower-left, leading line of her arm points to the carafe.
- **Facial Expression:** (partial profile glimpsed past cheek) calm, eyes forward and down toward the carafe, lashes lowered, lips softly closed.
- **Object Interaction:** her hand opens toward the carafe handle, fingers spreading in anticipation of the grip.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:03–0:05 camera arcs gently around her right shoulder, holding the OTS as she reaches.
- **Subject Action:** 0:03–0:04 she steps in, weight transfers onto the front foot; 0:04–0:05 right arm extends, hand reaches the carafe handle.
- **Object Action:** carafe still; steam continues curling; the loose hair strand sways forward as she leans.
- **Physics:** silk pulls taut across the shoulder blades on the reach then releases; ponytail swings with a slight delay and settles; realistic arm-extension muscle tension.
- **Object Interaction:** 0:05 fingers close on the brass handle — believable wrap, knuckle flex, contact shadow under fingers, no clipping through the handle.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:03 soft focus forward; 0:04 a small downward eye-settle on the target; 0:05 a feather-light single blink as the grip lands.
- **Lighting Behavior:** as the camera arcs, the sun rim sweeps across her ponytail like a moving highlight.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus held on the carafe; her shoulder stays soft foreground bokeh.
- **Diegetic Sound:** soft barefoot step on oak; faint fabric shift; a light brass-handle tap as fingers meet it; continuous low city hum and room tone.
- **Loop note:** —

---

### FRAME 3 — profile | medium | side pose | slight low angle
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, clean side profile, lifting the carafe and tilting it toward the waiting cup.
- **Hairstyle:** ponytail in full side silhouette, sleek crown, the loose strand grazing her cheekbone.
- **Wardrobe:** silk shirt-dress in profile, sleeve rolled at the forearm, belt catching a glint.
- **Footwear:** barefoot, weight even.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** hoop earring framed clean against the bright window; watch face catching sun; glossy nails on the carafe.
- **Pose & Framing:** pure side pose, medium framing (waist up), profile reading the jaw-neck-shoulder line crisply.
- **Camera:** slight low angle, 50mm, profile-on; window light blazing behind creating a luminous edge.
- **Background (powerful):** blown-out luminous skyline behind glass, the orange flower a soft vivid blur, brass and marble glints.
- **Lighting:** strong contre-jour rim along her profile (nose, lips, lash, ponytail all edge-lit gold); gentle fill on the near cheek to keep skin detail.
- **Color & Vibrance:** golden rim against rich mid-tone skin, saturated warm overall, cool sky sliver for balance.
- **Composition:** profile facing frame-right toward the cup, carafe raised upper-center, negative space of bright window left.
- **Facial Expression:** focused calm, eyes tracking the pour-point, a serene micro-smile, lips just barely parted in soft concentration.
- **Object Interaction:** both elements held with control — carafe tilted at a believable pour angle above the cup, wrist relaxed.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:05–0:07 slow lateral track staying locked on the profile, a hair of low-angle rise.
- **Subject Action:** 0:05–0:06 she raises the carafe and angles her wrist to begin the pour; 0:06–0:07 settles into a held, graceful pour stance.
- **Object Action:** 0:06 the first dark coffee stream leaves the carafe spout — then **the impossible begins**: instead of falling, the stream **hesitates and curves upward**, drawn toward the cup-then-back-to-carafe path in defiance of gravity (the hero move seeds here).
- **Physics:** liquid reads as real coffee — correct dark viscosity, surface sheen, ribbon thickness — but its gravity vector is inverted: it flows up in a smooth arc with believable fluid dynamics (stretch, surface tension beads, no splatter). Steam still rises normally, selling the contrast.
- **Object Interaction:** carafe handle grip stays perfect through the tilt; wrist counter-rotates naturally to hold the angle.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:05 eyes lead down to the spout; 0:06 calm focus, the faint smile holds; 0:07 a slow, unbothered blink — she does not react to the impossible. That non-reaction is the joke.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the rising coffee ribbon catches the contre-jour sun, glowing amber at its edges.
- **Lens / Optical:** subtle focus pull from her eye to the coffee ribbon as it starts to rise.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the soft glug-and-pour of coffee but played in a gently *reversed* timbre to sell the upward flow; carafe tilt creak; a tiny liquid-bead tick; continuous room tone.
- **Loop note:** —

---

### FRAME 4 — three-quarter front | medium close-up | 3/4 pose | eye-level push
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, three-quarter toward camera, watching the impossible pour with serene indifference.
- **Hairstyle:** ponytail crown and face-framing strand, glossy flyaway-free finish, baby-hairs catching light.
- **Wardrobe:** silk collar and open neckline, gold chain belt glint at lower frame.
- **Footwear:** out of frame.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** hoops, stacked rings on the carafe hand, glossy nails, watch.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter pose, medium close-up (chest up), face the clear hero of the frame.
- **Camera:** eye-level, slight push-in, 85mm portrait compression, shallow focus.
- **Background (powerful):** the rising coffee ribbon arcs through the upper frame, vivid skyline bokeh behind, orange flower a saturated blur.
- **Lighting:** soft beauty key from window-left, warm fill, gentle catch-light in both eyes, hair rim gold.
- **Color & Vibrance:** glowing warm skin, the dark coffee ribbon a rich contrast, saturated bokeh — punchy and clean.
- **Composition:** face right-of-center, coffee ribbon as a leading diagonal from her cup-hand up through negative space.
- **Facial Expression (heavily detailed):** lids relaxed three-quarter, eyes softly tracking the floating ribbon without surprise; brow smooth; the corner-smile alive; lips barely parted; the whole face fluid and breathing, not posed.
- **Object Interaction:** cup held steady in the near hand, thumb along its rim.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:07–0:09 slow push-in to the medium close-up, easing to a near-still hold.
- **Subject Action:** 0:07–0:08 she lifts her chin a fraction to follow the ribbon; 0:08–0:09 a tiny, almost-amused tilt of the head — the only acknowledgement.
- **Object Action:** the coffee ribbon completes its upward arc, threading from cup back into the carafe in a continuous glowing loop of liquid.
- **Physics:** the liquid loop holds laminar flow, edges beading with surface tension, catching light; her ponytail sways softly as she tilts; silk shifts with breath.
- **Object Interaction:** cup stays level with believable micro-adjustments of the wrist; no spill, contact shadow under thumb.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:07 eyes lead up-tracking the ribbon; 0:08 mouth corner lifts a hair (the wink-less wink); 0:09 a slow savoring blink, breath out — serene.
- **Lighting Behavior:** catch-lights in her eyes brighten as the push-in lands; ribbon glow throws a faint warm bounce on her cheek.
- **Lens / Optical:** shallow 85mm focus pins her eyes; ribbon and skyline melt to creamy bokeh.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the reversed-pour timbre peaks softly; a delicate liquid-thread shimmer; her quiet breath; intimate room tone.
- **Loop note:** —

---

### FRAME 5 — overhead / top-down | medium | overhead pose | high angle
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, seen from directly above, looking up toward the lens past the floating coffee loop.
- **Hairstyle:** the ponytail spirals out behind her crown in a clean graphic line from the top-down view, part razor-crisp.
- **Wardrobe:** silk shirt-dress shoulders and neckline read as soft folds from above, belt a gold line.
- **Footwear:** bare feet small at the bottom of frame on warm oak.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** hoops, rings, glossy nails framing the carafe and cup from above.
- **Pose & Framing:** overhead pose, medium framing, her upturned face center, the carafe-cup-ribbon loop a perfect circle of liquid around the lower frame.
- **Camera:** top-down high angle, 35mm, looking straight down.
- **Background (powerful):** the oak floor and marble island become a graphic backdrop; the vibrant orange flower lies as a bold color burst in the corner.
- **Lighting:** soft top ambient plus the window glow raking across the floor; her face lit upward by warm bounce.
- **Color & Vibrance:** warm oak + creamy marble + the saturated orange + the dark glossy coffee loop — rich and graphic.
- **Composition:** strong radial symmetry, the liquid loop encircling the lower third, her face the calm center.
- **Facial Expression:** looking up into lens, serene and direct, a slow soft smile, eyes calm and bright, utterly unbothered.
- **Object Interaction:** carafe in one hand, cup in the other, both held at the perfect distance to sustain the floating loop.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:09–0:11 a slow overhead rotation (gentle clockwise spin) above her.
- **Subject Action:** 0:09–0:10 she tilts her face up toward the spinning lens; 0:10–0:11 holds the gaze, the faint smile blooming a touch.
- **Object Action:** the coffee loop keeps cycling, now subtly spiraling with the camera rotation; steam threads upward through the center.
- **Physics:** the liquid loop maintains continuous flow under the rotation, droplets orbiting with believable centripetal lean; ponytail fans on the floor and shifts with her micro-movements.
- **Object Interaction:** both hands hold carafe and cup rock-steady through the spin, wrists relaxed, no wobble that would break the loop.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:09 eyes find the lens; 0:10 corner-smile grows, a slow blink; 0:11 calm hold, soft breath.
- **Lighting Behavior:** as the camera spins, the window glow sweeps across her face like a slow rotating light.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus locked on her face; floor and loop softly sharp around her.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the reversed-pour loop hum steadies into a soft musical tone; a gentle airy whoosh of the rotation; quiet breath; room tone.
- **Loop note:** —

---

### FRAME 6 — low angle hero | medium-full | front pose | low angle
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, low-angle hero shot, standing tall and calm with the floating coffee loop beside her like it's the most normal thing in the world.
- **Hairstyle:** ponytail towering in the low angle, glossy and sculptural against the bright glass.
- **Wardrobe:** silk shirt-dress flowing from the low view, hem catching a breeze, belt glinting.
- **Footwear:** bare feet planted, ankle chain visible, low angle elongating the stance.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** hoops, rings, watch, glossy nails — all catching warm light.
- **Pose & Framing:** powerful front pose, medium-full (knees up), heroic stance, the loop floating to her side.
- **Camera:** low angle looking up, 28mm, slight wide grandeur, the skyline towering behind glass.
- **Background (powerful):** the full sunrise skyline and cloud-sea blaze above and behind her, sun flaring at the glass edge, the orange flower a vivid accent low in frame.
- **Lighting:** dramatic backlit sun halo, strong rim, warm uplight bounce on her face and the underside of the loop.
- **Color & Vibrance:** maximum golden-hour saturation, glowing rim, deep contrast — the hero vibrance frame.
- **Composition:** Aira commanding center, coffee loop frame-left at chest height, sun flare upper-right.
- **Facial Expression:** confident calm, chin level, eyes soft on the lens, the knowing corner-smile at its fullest — quietly powerful.
- **Object Interaction:** she lets go of the cup mid-air for a beat — it hangs, held by the loop — while her hand opens, palm up, effortless.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:11–0:13 the camera cranes down to the low hero angle and pushes in slightly.
- **Subject Action:** 0:11–0:12 she straightens, shoulders settling back; 0:12–0:13 opens her free hand palm-up beside the floating cup, letting it hover.
- **Object Action:** the cup hovers, suspended by the looping coffee; the ribbon glows; steam rises straight up; her silk hem lifts in a soft draft.
- **Physics:** the released cup holds with a believable tiny bob as if buoyed; silk hem flutter has real fabric weight and delayed motion; sun flare blooms optically.
- **Object Interaction:** the hand release is clean — fingers uncurl smoothly, the cup neither drops nor jerks, contact transfers seamlessly to the levitating loop.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:11 eyes to lens; 0:12 corner-smile blooms; 0:13 a slow assured blink and breath — soft-power hero beat.
- **Lighting Behavior:** sun flare swells as the camera lands low, rim light intensifying around her whole silhouette.
- **Lens / Optical:** anamorphic-style flare streak across frame; focus holds her, flare softening the edges.
- **Diegetic Sound:** a swelling warm tone as the cup releases; the soft musical hum of the loop; a gentle draft whoosh through silk; her calm breath.
- **Loop note:** —

---

### FRAME 7 — return to wide | wide | full body | front pose | eye-level (LOOP CLOSE)
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, returned to the exact opening stance at the island, carafe and cup settling back to their start positions.
- **Hairstyle:** glossy high ponytail, identical to Frame 1.
- **Wardrobe:** ivory silk shirt-dress, gold belt — matching Frame 1 exactly.
- **Footwear:** barefoot, ankle chain, same relaxed stance.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** hoops, rings, watch, glossy nails — continuity-matched.
- **Pose & Framing:** full-body front pose, right third of frame — a mirror of Frame 1 for a seamless loop.
- **Camera:** eye-level 35mm, the same establishing composition as Frame 1.
- **Background (powerful):** the sunrise skyline and cloud-sea, warm gold flood, vivid orange flower — matched to opening.
- **Lighting:** identical sunrise key/fill/rim to Frame 1.
- **Color & Vibrance:** matched saturated golden palette.
- **Composition:** identical to Frame 1 so the cut loops invisibly.
- **Facial Expression:** serene, faint corner-smile, relaxed lids — the exact resting face of Frame 1.
- **Object Interaction:** fingertips rest on the marble, carafe and cup back at start position, ready to pour again.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:13–0:15 the camera eases back out to the opening wide and settles to a still hold matching Frame 1.
- **Subject Action:** 0:13–0:14 she lowers the carafe to the island and rests her fingertips on the marble; 0:14–0:15 a calm breath, returning to the opening pose.
- **Object Action:** the coffee loop gently lowers the cup back to its saucer; the liquid settles into the cup normally; steam resumes lazy curls — everything reset.
- **Physics:** the cup lands with a soft believable weight and tiny rock; coffee surface ripples once and stills; silk and ponytail settle to rest.
- **Object Interaction:** carafe placed down with perfect soft contact (base meets marble, faint flex), cup re-seated on saucer cleanly.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:13 eyes ease forward; 0:14 corner-smile resets to resting; 0:15 slow blink, breath out — matched to Frame 1's first beat for the loop.
- **Lighting Behavior:** sunrise glow steadies to the opening level.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus settles to the deep opening look.
- **Diegetic Sound:** soft ceramic settle of cup on saucer; faint coffee-surface ripple; one slow breath; the distant city hum returning to the Frame 1 bed — looping cleanly.
- **Loop note:** **LOOP POINT** — positions, light, and expression match Frame 1 exactly for a seamless repeat.

---

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — A-1 (background music / sound bed)
*Use this as the underscore laid beneath the cut — separate from the diegetic sounds inside the prompts.*

- **Genre / vibe:** warm, dreamy lo-fi morning groove with a luxe edge — slow, glossy, unbothered.
- **Tempo / key:** ~70 BPM, warm major key (A or C), relaxed swing.
- **Core elements:** soft Rhodes electric-piano chords; a round muted upright-bass pulse; brushed/soft finger-snap percussion; a faint vinyl-warmth crackle; a high airy pad shimmer for the "magic" glow.
- **Arc:** gentle intro on Frames 1–2 (Rhodes + room) → bass and snaps enter as she reaches (Frame 2–3) → a soft shimmer swell on the impossible pour (Frame 3–4) → fullest warmth at the low-angle hero (Frame 6) → settle back to the intro texture on the loop close (Frame 7) so the audio loops seamlessly with the visual.
- **Texture note:** keep it low and supportive so the reversed-pour and liquid-loop diegetic sounds still read on top.
- **Loop:** must be a clean 15s loop matching the visual loop point.
```



## CONCEPT A-2 — "Every Floor's a Different World"

- **Feeling:** wonder / surprise
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** voluminous glossy blunt bob, deep side part, soft inward curl at the jaw, high shine
- **Magic move:** each elevator *ding* opens the doors onto a completely different impossible world; Aira leans on the rail, unbothered, like it's her daily commute
- **Concept line:** "every floor's a different life"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move inside a mirrored elevator, 7 frames, the camera circling as the doors keep revealing new worlds
- **Loop:** final doors close on the same world that opened in Frame 1

---

### FRAME 1 — establishing | medium-full | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, leaning one shoulder against a mirrored elevator wall, ankles crossed, completely relaxed.
- **Hairstyle:** voluminous glossy blunt bob, deep side part, inward jaw-curl, mirror-shine.
- **Wardrobe:** a structured cobalt-blue power-suit blazer over a silk camisole, wide-leg trousers, sharp tailoring.
- **Footwear:** glossy black pointed-toe heels, thin ankle strap.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** oversized tortoise-shell sunglasses pushed up on the head, gold statement ear-cuff, sleek black structured handbag held loose, deep-red glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter pose, medium-full (knees up), she anchors the left third, the elevator doors fill center-right.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, the mirrored walls multiplying soft reflections for depth.
- **Background (powerful):** a sleek brushed-steel-and-mirror elevator interior, warm recessed ceiling light, a glowing floor-number display reading shifting digits; through the doors (closed) a thin seam of bright light.
- **Lighting:** soft top key, warm bounce off brushed steel, a cool rim from the door seam, mirror reflections doubling highlights.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated cobalt suit as the color anchor against warm steel and deep-red nails — punchy, glossy, rich blacks.

- **Composition:** Aira left third, mirrored reflections receding right, the closed doors as the focal "stage curtain."
- **Facial Expression:** serene boredom — lids three-quarter, a faint patient half-smile, eyes calm, the look of someone who's seen it all before.
- **Object Interaction:** handbag hangs from a relaxed crooked elbow, fingertips of the free hand resting on the cool steel rail.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 slow push-in toward the doors from the medium-full.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 a slow breath, weight settling on the leaning shoulder; 0:01–0:02 her eyes flick up to the floor-number display.
- **Object Action:** the floor-number digits tick upward with a soft glow; the door seam brightens.
- **Physics:** the bob sways with a soft delayed weight as she settles; blazer fabric holds structured folds; handbag micro-swings on the elbow.
- **Object Interaction:** fingertips keep believable contact on the rail — slight skin flatten, no float.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 calm, slow blink; 0:01 eyes lead up to the display; 0:02 patient half-smile holds, soft exhale.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the door seam glows brighter as the elevator "arrives," cool light leaking onto her cheek.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus eases from her to the doors as the push-in lands.
- **Diegetic Sound:** soft elevator hum; a gentle mechanical rise; a muffled musical *ding* approaching; faint fabric shift; one slow breath.
- **Loop note:** this is the world the final doors will close on.

---

### FRAME 2 — over-the-shoulder | medium | back/OTS pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, seen over her shoulder from behind as the doors part onto an **underwater coral city** — glowing reefs, drifting rays of light, schools of neon fish — held back by invisible glass, water never spilling in.
- **Hairstyle:** blunt bob from behind, deep part sharp, glossy nape.
- **Wardrobe:** cobalt blazer shoulders and back drape, camisole strap glint.
- **Footwear:** out of frame.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** ear-cuff catching the aqua glow, sunglasses still perched on the crown.
- **Pose & Framing:** back/OTS pose, medium (waist up), her shoulder frames lower-left, the underwater world blazing through the open doors.
- **Camera:** eye-level behind her, 50mm, she is soft foreground, the reef is the sharp subject.
- **Background (powerful):** a vast bioluminescent coral metropolis — towering glowing corals, god-rays piercing teal water, schools of electric-blue and magenta fish, a whale silhouette far in the haze.
- **Lighting:** intense aqua glow washing back over her shoulder, cool rim on the bob, warm elevator light on her near side for contrast.
- **Color & Vibrance:** electric teal + magenta + glowing coral orange — maximum saturated fantasy color against her cobalt suit.
- **Composition:** OTS, her dark shoulder anchoring the vivid reveal, god-rays as leading lines into depth.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — A-2 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** sleek, mysterious deep-house / cinematic travel groove — cool, glossy, effortlessly confident.
- **Tempo / key:** ~110 BPM, minor key (F#m), hypnotic four-on-the-floor pulse kept low.
- **Core elements:** deep sub-bass; a soft filtered house kick; a shimmering arpeggiated synth that "travels"; airy vocal-chop pads; a soft elevator-chime motif echoed musically on each world-reveal.
- **Arc:** minimal pulse on Frame 1 → arp opens as the first world appears (Frame 2) → each world-reveal adds a new textural layer (water shimmer, petal-bells, neon synth-stabs, desert wind-pad) → fullest at the desert hero (Frame 5) → strips back to the minimal pulse on the loop close (Frame 6).
- **Texture note:** keep mids open so each world's diegetic ambience cuts through.
- **Loop:** clean 12s loop matching the visual loop point.
```


## CONCEPT A-3 — "Rain Falls Up"

- **Feeling:** dreamy delight / surprise
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** long sleek wet-look waves, center part, glossy and damp, tucked behind one ear
- **Magic move:** rain lifts **upward** — drops rise from the puddles back into the sky — and Aira strolls through it, umbrella open, unbothered
- **Concept line:** "everything finds its way back up"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken glide down a rain-soaked old-town street at blue hour, 6 frames flowing as a single travel
- **Loop:** final frame returns her to the opening doorway, umbrella tilt matched

---

### FRAME 1 — establishing | wide | full body | front pose | low eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, stepping out of a warm-lit doorway onto a wet cobblestone street, umbrella half-raised, mid-stride and serene.
- **Hairstyle:** long sleek wet-look waves, center part, glossy, one side tucked behind the ear.
- **Wardrobe:** a belted emerald-green trench coat, sharp collar up, over a black turtleneck; the coat catching the wet sheen of the light.
- **Footwear:** glossy oxblood ankle boots, slim heel, reflecting in the wet stones.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** a transparent dome umbrella with a gold handle, small gold drop earrings, a thin gold chain, deep-plum glossy nails on the umbrella handle.
- **Pose & Framing:** full-body front pose, slight three-quarter stride, she occupies center-right, head-to-boots in frame, reflected in the wet cobbles.
- **Camera:** low eye-level, 35mm, deep focus reading the whole street.
- **Background (powerful):** a romantic European old-town alley at blue hour — leaning timber-and-stone buildings, glowing amber shop windows, strings of warm bistro bulbs, a wet cobble street mirroring every light, a cathedral spire in the misty distance.
- **Lighting:** cool blue-hour ambient key; warm amber practicals from shop windows and bulbs; rim from a streetlamp; the wet ground bouncing colored reflections.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated emerald coat + warm amber lights + cool blue dusk + oxblood boots — rich, glossy, cinematic, deep blacks.

- **Composition:** Aira center-right in the doorway light, the alley receding as a leading line to the distant spire, reflections doubling the scene below.
- **Facial Expression:** calm and content, lids relaxed, a soft secret smile in the corners, eyes taking in the street — at home in the rain.
- **Object Interaction:** her plum-nailed hand grips the gold umbrella handle with relaxed control, the dome tilted just off her shoulder.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:03 slow push-in and gentle dolly-forward following her first steps.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she steps down from the doorway, weight transferring; 0:01–0:03 begins a slow stroll, umbrella settling overhead.
- **Object Action:** rain falls — then **reverses**: drops on the cobbles lift and rise upward past the dome toward the sky; shop bulbs sway gently.
- **Physics:** the rising raindrops keep correct water behavior (streak, bead, sheen) but with an inverted gravity vector — smooth upward acceleration, tiny trailing tails; trench hem and wet hair sway with real weight; puddle reflections ripple as drops leave them.
- **Object Interaction:** her grip on the handle stays perfect through the step; the dome holds a believable tilt, drops curving up around its rim.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 calm, slow blink; 0:01 eyes lead up to a rising drop; 0:02–0:03 secret smile deepens, soft breath.
- **Lighting Behavior:** amber window light flickers across her as she passes; wet rim light slides along the coat.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus eases from the doorway to the street as she advances; bokeh of rising drops sparkling.
- **Diegetic Sound:** rain ambience played with a gentle reversed shimmer for the upward flow; soft boot-steps on wet stone; distant muffled café chatter; a far church bell; her quiet breath.
- **Loop note:** doorway position is the master reference for the final frame.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:11–0:13 camera eases back out to the opening wide and settles to a still hold matching Frame 1.
- **Subject Action:** 0:11–0:12 she steps back up into the doorway; 0:12–0:13 resettles into the opening half-raised stance, a calm breath.
- **Object Action:** rising rain steadies to the gentle opening rhythm; bulbs sway softly; reflections still.
- **Physics:** trench and wet hair settle with soft delayed weight; umbrella holds the opening tilt.
- **Object Interaction:** her grip resettles on the handle with believable soft contact; boots re-meet the doorstep cleanly.

- **Lens / Optical:** focus settles to the deep opening look.
- **Diegetic Sound:** soft boot-step onto the doorstep; reversed-rain shimmer returning to the Frame 1 bed; distant café murmur; one slow breath — looping cleanly.
- **Loop note:** **LOOP POINT** — positions, light, and expression match Frame 1 exactly.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — A-3 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** romantic cinematic lo-fi with a rainy-jazz warmth — wistful, dreamy, glossy.
- **Tempo / key:** ~75 BPM, warm minor-major blend (Dm to F), gentle swing.
- **Core elements:** soft jazz piano; brushed snare; warm upright bass; a faint accordion/strings pad for the European-street romance; a high glassy shimmer for the rising rain; subtle vinyl rain-crackle.
- **Arc:** intimate piano on Frames 1–2 → bass and brushes enter on the stroll → a glassy shimmer swell at the look-up wonder (Frame 3) → fullest warmth at the low-angle hero (Frame 5) → settle back to solo piano on the loop close (Frame 6).
- **Texture note:** keep low and warm so the reversed-rain shimmer reads on top.
- **Loop:** clean 13s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT A-4 — "I Set the Mood"

- **Feeling:** playful power / surprise
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** sculptural sleek low bun, razor-sharp middle part, polished and glassy, fully off the face
- **Magic move:** a wall dimmer controls the **actual sky** outside the window — one slow turn cycles day → sunset → night → dawn — and Aira treats it like adjusting a thermostat
- **Concept line:** "I set the mood"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move through a brutalist concrete loft with a colossal arched window, 6 frames
- **Loop:** final turn of the dimmer returns the sky to the exact opening daylight

---

### FRAME 1 — establishing | wide | full body | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, standing beside a minimalist brass wall-dimmer, hand raised to it, poised and unbothered.
- **Hairstyle:** sculptural sleek low bun, razor middle part, glassy polish, off the face.
- **Wardrobe:** a draped oatmeal-and-rust color-blocked knit gown, one shoulder bare, soft sculptural folds, floor-length.
- **Footwear:** barefoot on polished concrete, a single gold toe-ring, relaxed stance.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** a bold sculptural gold cuff bracelet, geometric gold earrings, warm terracotta glossy nails, no eyewear.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter pose, full body, she anchors the right third, the colossal window dominating left-center.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus reading the vast room.
- **Background (powerful):** a cathedral-scale brutalist concrete loft — a single colossal arched window framing an epic alpine valley at midday, snow peaks, a turquoise glacial lake far below, raw concrete, one rust-toned modular sofa, a tall vivid monstera as the green color anchor.
- **Lighting:** bright midday daylight flooding through the arch (cool-neutral key); warm bounce off concrete; soft fill; rim on her bun and bare shoulder.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated turquoise lake + rust gown + vivid green monstera against warm concrete — rich, clean, deep shadows.

- **Composition:** Aira right third at the dimmer, the arched window and alpine vista filling the rest, leading the eye out to the peaks.
- **Facial Expression:** serene authority — lids relaxed, a faint knowing smile, eyes calm on the window like she owns the sky.
- **Object Interaction:** terracotta-nailed fingertips rest on the brass dimmer knob, poised to turn it.

**VIDEO PROMPT**

- **Object Action:** the alpine sky sits bright at midday; the monstera leaves drift faintly in an AC breeze.

- **Object Interaction:** fingertips meet the brass knob with perfect soft contact, slight skin flatten, ready to rotate.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 calm, slow blink; 0:01 eyes lead to the window; 0:02–0:03 knowing smile holds, soft exhale.
- **Lighting Behavior:** midday light steady and bright across the concrete.

## CONCEPT A-5 — "I Don't Lift a Finger"

- **Feeling:** breezy delight / surprise
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a glossy braided halo crown wrapped around the head, a few soft face-framing tendrils left loose
- **Magic move:** a bag of groceries **puts itself away** — fruit, jars and bottles float out and glide into their exact places in a choreographed ballet — while Aira just leans on the counter and watches
- **Concept line:** "I don't lift a finger"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move through a sun-drenched coastal kitchen, 6 frames
- **Loop:** final frame returns the bag to the counter, full and upright, ready to unpack again

---

### FRAME 1 — establishing | wide | full body | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, setting a brown paper grocery bag onto a marble island, one hip leaning in, easy and relaxed.
- **Hairstyle:** glossy braided halo crown, soft face-framing tendrils loose.
- **Wardrobe:** a breezy buttercup-yellow linen wrap dress, three-quarter sleeves, soft sash tie at the waist.
- **Footwear:** flat tan leather sandals with a thin ankle tie, a delicate gold anklet.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** small gold studs, a thin gold bangle stack, a fine gold necklace, soft coral glossy nails, no eyewear.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter pose, full body, she anchors the right third, the open kitchen and ocean window filling left-center.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus reading the whole bright kitchen.
- **Background (powerful):** a sun-drenched coastal kitchen with a colossal open window framing a turquoise ocean and white cliffs, pale travertine and warm oak cabinetry, brass open shelves, a big bowl of vivid citrus and a vase of fresh blue hydrangeas as color anchors.
- **Lighting:** bright airy seaside daylight key from the window, warm bounce off travertine, soft fill, gentle rim on the braid crown.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated turquoise ocean + buttercup dress + vivid citrus orange + hydrangea blue — fresh, bright, glossy, clean shadows.

- **Composition:** Aira right third at the island, the ocean window and citrus bowl leading the eye, brass shelves framing the future float-path.
- **Facial Expression:** light and content — lids relaxed, an easy soft smile, eyes on the bag like she already knows what happens next.
- **Object Interaction:** both coral-nailed hands settle the paper bag onto the marble with believable weight, then release.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:03 slow push-in from the wide toward the bag on the island.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she lowers the bag and lets go; 0:01–0:03 leans a hip on the counter, folds her arms loosely, settling in to watch.
- **Object Action:** the paper bag settles; a citrus rolls slightly; then the topmost lemon lifts and begins to float — the magic seeds here.
- **Physics:** paper bag crinkles and settles with believable weight; the lifting lemon rises smoothly with correct mass and a gentle bob; linen dress sways with soft drape; tendrils float in the sea breeze.
- **Object Interaction:** her hands release the bag cleanly, fingers uncurling, contact transferring to the marble; then arms fold with relaxed ease.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 calm, slow blink; 0:01 eyes lead to the bag; 0:02–0:03 easy smile, soft exhale.
- **Lighting Behavior:** bright sea light steady; faint sun-sparkle off the ocean reflecting on the ceiling.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus eases from her to the bag as the push-in lands.
- **Diegetic Sound:** soft paper-bag set-down and crinkle; gentle ocean waves and gulls through the window; a light sea breeze; one easy breath.
- **Loop note:** bag position and fullness are the master reference for the final frame.

- **Background (powerful):** the kitchen and ocean window melting to warm bokeh, floating items as soft shapes, citrus glow.

- **Color & Vibrance:** glowing warm skin, buttercup and coral accents, turquoise bokeh — fresh and punchy.
- **Composition:** face right-of-center, the cherry on a leading diagonal toward her lips.
- **Facial Expression (heavily detailed):** playful contentment — lids relaxed, eyes flicking from the cherry to the lens, lips parting in a soft anticipatory smile, fluid and breathing.
- **Object Interaction:** coral-nailed fingers pinch the cherry stem with perfect delicate control, plucking it from its float-path.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:07–0:09 slow push-in to the medium close-up, easing to a near-still hold.
- **Subject Action:** 0:07–0:08 she reaches up and pinches a floating cherry; 0:08–0:09 draws it toward her lips with a playful glance to the lens.
- **Object Action:** the plucked cherry leaves the orbit; the rest of the ballet continues softly behind her.
- **Physics:** the cherry has believable small mass; its stem bends slightly as she pinches; other items keep orbiting; tendrils float.
- **Object Interaction:** finger-to-stem pinch is precise — the cherry detaches cleanly from its float and tracks exactly with her fingers.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:07 eyes lead up to the cherry; 0:08 a playful flick to lens, lips part; 0:09 a slow savoring near-bite pause, soft breath.
- **Lighting Behavior:** catch-lights brighten as the push-in lands; cherry gloss catches a highlight.
- **Lens / Optical:** shallow 85mm pins her eyes and the cherry; background melts to bokeh.
- **Diegetic Sound:** a tiny pluck; soft orbit whooshes behind; ocean ambience; her playful breath.
- **Loop note:** —

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — A-5 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** breezy bossa-nova / sunlit french-pop groove — light, glossy, effortlessly happy.
- **Tempo / key:** ~100 BPM, bright major key (G), gentle bossa sway.
- **Core elements:** soft nylon-string guitar; brushed bossa drums; a round upright bass; light vibraphone twinkles for the floating items; a faint whistle/hum melody; a sun-warm string pad.
- **Arc:** easy guitar on Frame 1 → vibraphone twinkles enter as groceries take flight (Frames 2–3) → fullest sunlit groove at the low-angle hero (Frame 5) → settle back to solo guitar on the loop close (Frame 6).
- **Texture note:** keep light and bouncy so the per-item whooshes and landing taps read on top.
- **Loop:** clean 13s loop matching the visual loop point.

---

# IDEA B — THE WORLD REACTS TO HER MOOD
*Feeling: relatable. No mirror, no product — she's just living. The environment is her emotional weather made visible.*

## CONCEPT B-1 — "Monday Morning"

- **Feeling:** relatable frustration → satisfaction
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** messy high bun with loose strands falling, a sage-green velvet scrunchie barely holding, undone chic
- **Magic move:** the whole room physically **dims and sulks** when she's annoyed (flowers droop, colors drain) — then **blooms saturated** when she finds her groove
- **Concept line:** "even the room knows"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move through a maximalist apartment on a grey morning, 7 frames
- **Loop:** final frame returns the room to its moody grey opening state, ready to cycle

---

### FRAME 1 — establishing | full body | center-left of screen | 7 feet from camera | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, full body visible head-to-feet, positioned **center-left of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens**. She stands in a doorway mid-yawn, one hand on the frame, weight slouched to one hip — pure Monday energy.
- **Hairstyle:** messy high bun, loose strands falling around the face, sage-green velvet scrunchie barely holding.
- **Wardrobe:** oversized soft grey cashmere cardigan over a white ribbed tank and charcoal silk sleep shorts; the cardigan sliding off one shoulder.
- **Footwear:** chunky cream shearling slides, one foot half in, one bare heel showing.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** no eyewear; a single dainty gold sleep-necklace, tiny diamond stud earrings, bare nails (natural pink).
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front-facing with a slight three-quarter slouch, **center-left of frame**; the living room fills the right two-thirds.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, camera **7 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a maximalist apartment — velvet jewel-tone furniture (emerald sofa, rust armchair), tall monstera, stacked books, brass lamps — but everything is **desaturated and grey** as if the color has been sucked out. Flowers in a vase are visibly drooping. A rainy grey window. The room is *sulking*.
- **Lighting:** flat overcast grey key from the window; no warmth anywhere; a single dull practical lamp barely trying.
- **Color & Vibrance:** deliberately muted/grey — this is the one frame where vibrancy is suppressed to set up the contrast (the directive allows this for deliberate moody briefs). Only her skin reads warm.
- **Composition:** Aira center-left in the doorway, the grey room sprawling right, leading lines of the furniture pointing toward the window.
- **Facial Expression:** mid-yawn, eyes scrunched shut, brow creased, mouth wide in an honest yawn — raw, unguarded, no performance. The "I'm not ready" face.
- **Object Interaction:** her left hand grips the doorframe at shoulder height with a relaxed lean; the cardigan slides off the opposite shoulder with believable fabric droop.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:03 very slow dolly-in from 7 feet to 5 feet, gentle and unhurried.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 the yawn completes, jaw closing; 0:01–0:02 she shuffles one step in, the shearling slide scuffing; 0:02–0:03 she pauses, surveying the grey room.
- **Object Action:** the flowers in the vase droop further as she enters; the lamp flickers weakly; a book on the stack slides a millimeter as if sighing.
- **Physics:** cardigan drapes with real heavy-knit weight, sliding off the shoulder; the slide scuffs with believable friction; flower stems bend with organic weight; monstera leaves hang limp.
- **Object Interaction:** her grip on the doorframe has believable finger-spread and release as she lets go; the slide foot drags with correct floor friction.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 yawn closing, eyes still scrunched; 0:01 eyes open heavy-lidded, a flat "ugh" expression, lips pressed, brow low; 0:02–0:03 a slow resigned blink, exhale through the nose.
- **Lighting Behavior:** flat and unchanged — no warmth entering yet.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus, no rack, the whole grey scene legible.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the tail of a quiet yawn-sigh; a slide scuffing on wood floor; the weak lamp buzz; rain tapping the window; a distant muffled city hum; one heavy breath.
- **Loop note:** room grey state is the master reference for the final frame.

- **Object Interaction:** her thumb meets the button with perfect contact pressure; the mug handle sits naturally in her grip.

- **Lighting Behavior:** the room dims a hair further as her mood drops — the sulking intensifies.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus shifts from her shoulder to the dead machine button.
- **Diegetic Sound:** mug scrape on marble; the button press — a weak click then nothing; a faint electrical failure buzz; rain intensifying; her frustrated exhale.
- **Loop note:** —

### FRAME 4 — three-quarter body (knees up) | center-right of screen | 5 feet from camera | 3/4 pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, three-quarter body visible (knees up), positioned **center-right of screen**, approximately **5 feet from lens**. She pulls the cardigan back up onto her shoulder with a deliberate, self-gathering motion — and the room starts to respond.

- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter body (knees up), 3/4 pose with squared shoulders, **center-right**; the room fills the left — and it's beginning to bloom.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 40mm, **5 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** the same room but now **waking up** — the emerald sofa is regaining its color, the flowers are lifting, the monstera leaves are perking, warm gold light is creeping in from the window as if the clouds parted. Half the room is still grey, half is blooming — the transition caught mid-sweep.
- **Lighting:** warm gold light entering from the window, mixing with the remaining grey — a split-tone moment.
- **Color & Vibrance:** half-and-half — saturated emerald and rust returning on the left, fading grey on the right. The color follows *her mood*.
- **Composition:** Aira center-right, the bloom sweeping left-to-right behind her, the split visible.
- **Facial Expression:** the shift — lids opening wider, eyes brightening, the flat line of the mouth softening into the beginnings of a real smile. Brow relaxing. The "okay, I got this" turn.
- **Object Interaction:** one hand tightens the scrunchie (fingers twist the hair with precision); the other straightens the cardigan with a confident tug.

**VIDEO PROMPT**

- **Subject Action:** 0:07–0:08 she tightens the scrunchie with one hand, squares her shoulders; 0:08–0:09 drops her hands to her sides and takes a deep, deliberate breath in.
- **Object Action:** in sync with her breath in, the room explodes into color — flowers lift and open, the sofa saturates to rich emerald, the lamp ignites to a warm glow, the monstera leaves reach upward, sunlight floods through the window.
- **Physics:** flowers lift with organic stem-flex; leaves uncurl with believable elasticity; light spreads at the speed of a cloud clearing (fast but not instant); cardigan fabric responds to her squaring with correct drape physics.
- **Object Interaction:** scrunchie twist has precise finger-hair contact; the tug on the cardigan shows correct fabric tension and release.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:07 the "got this" look solidifying; 0:08 eyes brighten, brow lifts to relaxed-open; 0:09 the smile arrives — not a grin, a warm settled confidence. A slow satisfied blink.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the gold floods in, warm key replacing the grey; the room goes from flat to richly directional.
- **Lens / Optical:** the dolly-back reveals more room; the bloom is legible in expanding frame.
- **Diegetic Sound:** a satisfying deep breath in; a soft musical swell (the room responding); flowers lifting with a tiny rustle; the lamp click-on; a warm hum replacing the grey ambience; rain stopping.
- **Loop note:** —

- **Object Interaction:** her hand re-grips the doorframe with believable contact.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:13 the smile fades; 0:14 eyes heavy; 0:15 yawn begins — matched to Frame 1.
- **Lighting Behavior:** warm gold drains to flat grey, matching opening.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus returns to deep.
- **Diegetic Sound:** espresso pour fading; rain returning; the dull lamp buzz; her yawn beginning — looping cleanly.
- **Loop note:** **LOOP POINT** — positions, light, color, and expression match Frame 1 exactly.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — B-1 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** cinematic lo-fi with a dramatic emotional arc — starts grey and minimal, blooms into rich warmth.
- **Tempo / key:** ~80 BPM, starts in A minor (grey), modulates to A major (bloom) at the turn.
- **Core elements:** muted piano on the grey frames; a soft vinyl crackle; building warm strings and a felt-kick as the bloom happens; a satisfying bass drop at the hero frame; strips back to muted piano on the loop.
- **Arc:** minimal grey piano (Frames 1–3) → a swelling transition riser (Frame 4 turn) → full warm strings + bass + bright piano (Frames 5–6) → decay back to minimal grey piano (Frame 7 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the transition from muted to full should feel like a cloud clearing — not abrupt, but deeply satisfying.
- **Loop:** clean 15s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT B-2 — "She Walked In"

- **Feeling:** empowerment / "main character entered"
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** long straight jet-black curtain hair, center part, ends brushing the elbows, glass-shine
- **Magic move:** every surface and object in a café **turns to face her** the moment she enters — chairs pivot, flowers lean, lights brighten toward her — then snap back to normal when she sits
- **Concept line:** "she walked in"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move through a busy artisan café, 6 frames
- **Loop:** final frame returns everything to its neutral pre-entrance state

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | center of screen | 8 feet from camera | front pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, full body visible head-to-feet, positioned **dead center of screen**, approximately **8 feet from lens**. She pushes open a heavy glass café door mid-stride, stepping through, one hand on the brass handle.
- **Hairstyle:** long jet-black curtain hair, center part, glass-shine, ends swaying with the forward motion.
- **Wardrobe:** a sharply-cut ivory blazer over a fitted black silk turtleneck body-suit, high-waist charcoal tailored trousers, a thin black leather belt with a gold buckle.
- **Footwear:** pointed black patent stilettos, mid-stride, catching a floor reflection.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** black rectangular cat-eye sunglasses pushed up on the head; chunky gold chain necklace; a structured black leather micro-bag in the non-door hand; espresso-brown glossy almond nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front stride, **dead center**; the café interior fans out behind the glass door.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **8 feet back**, shooting from inside the café toward the door.
- **Background (powerful):** a high-ceilinged artisan café — exposed brick, warm oak tables, brass pendant lights, a long marble espresso bar, fresh eucalyptus sprigs in vases, patrons as soft blurs. Warm and textured.
- **Lighting:** warm interior key from the brass pendants; a slash of daylight through the opening door illuminating her from behind as a rim.
- **Color & Vibrance:** rich warm tones — ivory blazer pops against brick and oak; gold hardware punches; black accents ground it; espresso nail color echoes the café.
- **Composition:** Aira dead center, the door frame and café converging on her as leading lines, daylight rim creating a halo.
- **Facial Expression:** cool, arrived confidence — chin level, eyes behind the slightly tinted opening (she's removing the glasses next), lips in a relaxed closed-mouth power-calm, jaw soft but set. Not smiling yet — letting the room notice.
- **Object Interaction:** her right hand grips the heavy brass door handle with deliberate strength, knuckles defined; the door swings with believable weight; the micro-bag hangs from her left forearm with correct leather weight.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 static hold at 8 feet as she pushes through, then a slow dolly-back begins.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she pushes the door open, weight transferring forward mid-stride; 0:01–0:02 her first step into the café lands, heel clicking, hair swinging.
- **Object Action:** the moment her foot crosses the threshold — every object starts to **turn toward her**: chairs at nearby tables pivot 5–10 degrees; pendant lights swing gently toward her; eucalyptus in the nearest vase leans; a coffee cup on a table slowly rotates its handle toward her.
- **Physics:** door swings with correct heavy-glass inertia and hydraulic resistance; her hair follows the stride with realistic delay and swing-settle; chair pivots are slow, smooth, mechanical but organic — like magnetism; pendant lights swing with correct cable physics.
- **Object Interaction:** her hand releases the brass handle with a clean uncurl; the door continues on its closer.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 cool neutral, jaw set; 0:01 a micro-lift of the chin as she enters; 0:02 eyes begin a slow scan — the "I see you all" sweep.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the daylight rim narrows as the door closes behind her; warm interior takes over.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus; door-light flare narrows and fades.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the heavy door push (a whoosh and brass click); her heel striking wood floor — sharp, decisive; café ambience (murmur, clink, soft music); a subtle dramatic silence ripple as she enters — the room dips in volume for a beat.
- **Loop note:** this door-open state is the master reference.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — B-2 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** a slow-burn cinematic bass-driven groove — confident, magnetic, minimal but powerful. Think runway music meets film score.

- **Texture note:** keep stripped and confident — this track should feel like her walk has its own soundtrack.
- **Loop:** clean 12s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT B-3 — "The Music Changed"

- **Feeling:** playful / mood shift relatable
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** two low pigtail braids, glossy, tied with thin black silk ribbons, ends brushing her collarbone
- **Magic move:** when she changes the song on her phone, the **entire environment morphs** to match the genre — jazz turns the room moody and smoky, pop makes it bright and candy-colored, classical makes it regal and grand — all around her while she cooks
- **Concept line:** "the music changed everything"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move through a kitchen that shape-shifts, 7 frames
- **Loop:** final song-skip returns the kitchen to the exact opening state

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | right of screen | 7 feet from camera | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, full body visible head-to-feet, positioned **right of screen (right third)**, approximately **7 feet from lens**. She stands at a kitchen island mid-cooking, a phone propped on a small stand beside the cutting board, one hand reaching to skip a track.
- **Hairstyle:** two low pigtail braids, glossy black, thin silk ribbons, ends at the collarbone.
- **Wardrobe:** a fitted burnt-orange ribbed knit top with a scoop neck, high-waist wide-leg cream linen pants, a small linen apron tied at the waist.
- **Footwear:** simple white canvas slip-ons, clean, relaxed.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** no eyewear; thin gold hoops, a simple woven bracelet, warm berry glossy short nails, a wooden cooking spoon in the non-phone hand.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, three-quarter pose facing the island, **right third of screen**; the neutral kitchen fills the left two-thirds.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **7 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a clean, bright modern kitchen — white subway tile, open oak shelves with ceramics and cookbooks, a pot simmering on the stove, herbs in terracotta pots, warm afternoon light from a window, a simple bluetooth speaker on the counter. Neutral and warm — the "before" state.
- **Lighting:** warm afternoon daylight key from the window; soft fill; a warm practical glow from under-cabinet strips.
- **Color & Vibrance:** warm neutral — burnt orange top and berry nails as the saturated anchors, the rest clean and bright but not extreme.
- **Composition:** Aira right third, the neutral kitchen left, the phone as the focal action-point at center.
- **Facial Expression:** easy concentration — eyes on the phone, brow slightly furrowed in a "not this song" way, lips pressed in mild thought, one braid swinging as she reaches.
- **Object Interaction:** her right thumb hovers over the phone screen, about to tap skip; her left hand holds the wooden spoon loosely, resting on the counter.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 slow push-in from 7 to 6 feet toward the phone.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she leans toward the phone; 0:01–0:02 her thumb taps "skip" — decisive.
- **Object Action:** the pot simmers; herbs sway in a window draft; the phone screen changes tracks.
- **Physics:** braids swing with her lean (correct pendulum); the spoon rests with believable wood weight; the simmer has correct bubble physics.
- **Object Interaction:** thumb meets phone screen with exact glass-touch contact; spoon stays balanced on the counter edge.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 mild "not this" frown; 0:01 decision — the frown lifts; 0:02 anticipation — eyes brighten, brow lifts.
- **Lighting Behavior:** warm afternoon steady — about to change.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus racks from her face to the phone as the skip happens.
- **Diegetic Sound:** a simmering pot; a faint ending track; the phone tap; a beat of silence — then the new genre hits.
- **Loop note:** this neutral state is the master reference for the final frame.

### FRAME 3 — close-up (face + shoulders) | center of screen | 2 feet from camera | front pose | eye-level — POP TRANSITION
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, close-up face and shoulders, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **2 feet from lens**. She taps skip again — and the environment shifts mid-frame toward bright pop.
- **Hairstyle:** braids now catching vivid pink and cyan light.
- **Wardrobe:** same orange knit top, now lit vivid — almost neon in the new light.
- **Footwear:** out of frame.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** hoops reflecting pink light; berry nails on the phone screen; bracelet catching cyan.
- **Pose & Framing:** close-up (face + shoulders), front, **dead center**.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 85mm, shallow, **2 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** mid-morph — the jazz amber and blue dissolving into bright candy-pink and electric cyan, the haze clearing into clean bold color-block washes; confetti-like elements beginning to appear.
- **Lighting:** bright pop-colored key (pink one side, cyan the other); flat and even; high-key, no deep shadow.

- **Composition:** her face dead center; the color shift sweeping behind her like a wave.
- **Facial Expression (heavily detailed):** the mood snaps — her expression jumps from jazz-sultry to playful pop-energy: eyes widen, brows lift, a big genuine grin breaks open showing teeth, cheeks lift. She goes from "cool" to "fun" in one beat. The transition is fluid — one melts into the other without a hard cut.
- **Object Interaction:** her thumb taps the phone again — the screen bright and glossy under her nail.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:04–0:06 static hold at 2 feet, letting the morph happen around her.
- **Subject Action:** 0:04–0:05 her thumb taps skip; 0:05–0:06 her expression transforms — the grin arriving, shoulders lifting, she starts a head-bob to the new beat.

- **Physics:** confetti has correct light paper-drift; the color shift travels across surfaces believably (like a light wash sweeping); braids swing with her head-bob.
- **Object Interaction:** phone screen tap — exact glass contact, the track visibly changing.

- **Lens / Optical:** shallow holds her face; the color morph reads as a soft-focus wash.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the jazz track fading; the tap; a beat of silence; then a bright pop beat drops — synths, claps, an upbeat vocal hook; her delighted gasp.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — B-3 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** this concept IS about music — so the external audio block is a **medley that shifts genre with the kitchen morph**. It's the actual music she's "playing."
- **Tempo / key:** shifts — jazz section (~100 BPM, Bb minor, swing) → pop section (~120 BPM, C major, four-on-floor) → classical section (~70 BPM, D major, orchestral) → back to neutral ambient on the loop.
- **Core elements per section:**
  - Jazz: upright bass, brushed snares, muted trumpet solo, warm Rhodes.
  - Pop: bright synth chords, clap-snap beat, a catchy vocal-chop hook, bubbly bass.
  - Classical: full strings, harp arpeggios, french horn, a grand piano.
- **Arc:** ambient kitchen sounds on Frame 1 → jazz fills the room (Frame 2) → a brief silence on the skip → pop drops (Frames 3–4) → brief silence → classical swells (Frame 5) → the laugh breaks it (Frame 6) → returns to ambient kitchen on the loop close (Frame 7).
- **Texture note:** each genre section should sound complete and authentic, not parody — the joke is in the environment morphing, not in the music being ironic.
- **Loop:** clean 14s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT B-4 — "Don't Text Him Back"

- **Feeling:** deeply relatable / inner conflict humor
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a loose tousled French twist, pieces falling around the face deliberately, a single decorative gold hairpin
- **Magic move:** her phone **physically resists her** — it slides away from her reaching hand, the screen dims when she picks it up, the keyboard letters scramble — because even the world knows she shouldn't text back
- **Concept line:** "even my phone said no"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move on a sofa in a cozy apartment, 6 frames
- **Loop:** final frame returns to the exact opening pose with the phone buzzing again

---

### FRAME 1 — three-quarter body (knees up) | center of screen | 5 feet from camera | front pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, three-quarter body visible (knees up), positioned **center of screen**, approximately **5 feet from lens**. She's curled on a deep velvet sofa, a throw over her legs, phone face-up on the cushion beside her — it's just buzzed and the screen glows.

- **Wardrobe:** a soft oversized camel-colored cashmere sweater with a wide cowl neck, black silk lounge pants, cozy and chic.

- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** no eyewear; the gold hairpin, small pearl drop earrings, a thin gold bracelet, warm nude-pink glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter body, curled front-facing on the sofa, **center of screen**; the cozy room wraps around her.

- **Background (powerful):** a deeply cozy maximalist living room at evening — the velvet sofa in midnight-navy, stacked bookshelves, warm amber lamps, a candle flickering on a side-table, a rain-streaked window glowing with city lights, a soft sheepskin underfoot, dried eucalyptus in a vase. Rich and intimate.

- **Object Interaction:** one hand rests on her chest (surprised); the other is by her side, close to the phone but not reaching yet.

### FRAME 5 — full body | center-left of screen | 6 feet from camera | front pose | slight low angle (HERO — THE GIVE-UP)
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, full body head-to-feet, positioned **center-left of screen**, approximately **6 feet from lens**. She has accepted defeat — she tosses the phone face-down onto the sofa cushion, sinks back with dramatic finality, and the room visibly EXHALES (a warm glow pulse ripples outward as if relieved).
- **Hairstyle:** French twist now slightly more undone from the frustration, pieces framing the surrendered face beautifully.
- **Wardrobe:** camel sweater, silk pants, throw kicked aside — comfortable defeat.
- **Footwear:** barefoot, toe-ring, feet up on the sofa now.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** pearl earrings, gold hairpin, bracelet, nude-pink nails now resting on her own chest.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front, sunk deep into the sofa with dramatic surrender, **center-left**; the relieved room fills right.
- **Camera:** slight low angle (from floor level), 28mm, **6 feet from lens**, giving her the hero-frame even in surrender.
- **Background (powerful):** the room doing a "relief bloom" — the amber lamp brightening a notch, the candle flame standing tall and steady, the rain outside softening to a gentle patter, the dried eucalyptus seeming to straighten, a warm golden glow-pulse radiating from where the phone landed.
- **Lighting:** the warm glow-pulse as a hero light moment — amber swelling then settling to a rich steady warmth; the whole room one notch brighter and cozier than before.
- **Color & Vibrance:** maximum cozy saturation — warm amber, deep navy, camel gold, candlelight — the room rewarding her for giving up the text.
- **Composition:** Aira center-left in dramatic surrender, the glow-pulse radiating from the phone outward, the room wrapping around her like a hug.
- **Facial Expression (heavily detailed):** dramatic surrender melting into genuine relief and private amusement — first: eyes closed, brow furrowed in theatrical defeat, mouth in a dramatic pout, chin lifted as if saying "fine." Then: the pout cracks into a small real smile — one corner pulling up despite herself, eyes still closed, brow softening. She knows the phone was right. Fluid melt from drama to acceptance.
- **Object Interaction:** the phone lands face-down on the cushion (tossed, not placed); her hands fold on her chest in surrender; the throw settles around her.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:08–0:10 static at the low angle, holding the hero-frame.
- **Subject Action:** 0:08–0:09 she tosses the phone and sinks back dramatically, eyes shutting; 0:09–0:10 the dramatic pout cracks into the private smile — she can't help it.
- **Object Action:** the phone lands face-down with a soft thud; the glow-pulse ripples outward from it (the room's sigh of relief); lamp brightens; candle steadies; rain softens.
- **Physics:** phone toss has correct arc and landing weight on velvet (a bounce-settle); the glow-pulse travels across surfaces at light-speed but is visible as a warm wash; throw fabric settles around her with real drape.
- **Object Interaction:** the toss is clean — her fingers release, the phone rotates in the air, lands face-down with a soft velvet impact; her hands settle on her chest with natural folding.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:08 the dramatic pout and shut eyes; 0:09 one corner-smile breaking through; 0:10 the full private amusement — eyes still closed, both corners up, a gentle exhale-laugh through the nose.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the glow-pulse swells then settles to a richer steady warm — the room has relaxed.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus reads the whole glowing room; a soft warmth filter settling.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the phone toss and velvet-thud; the glow-pulse as a soft warm musical sigh (like a room exhaling); lamp brightening hum; rain softening; her dramatic sigh then the nose-laugh; candle crackle settling.
- **Loop note:** —

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — B-4 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** a warm, slightly comedic indie-pop groove — cozy, wry, relatable. Think "the soundtrack to overthinking at midnight."
- **Tempo / key:** ~88 BPM, warm major-minor blend (Em to G), gentle and wry.
- **Core elements:** soft plucked acoustic guitar; a quiet vinyl-crackle; muted pizzicato strings for the comedic tension; a gentle bass-pulse; a warm synth pad; a playful muted trumpet doing a "wah-wah" motif at the give-up.
- **Arc:** quiet guitar + crackle on Frame 1 (tension) → pizzicato strings enter on the phone-slide comedy (Frames 2–3) → the scramble-scene gets playful percussive taps (Frame 4) → a warm "wah-wah" and pad swell at the surrender (Frame 5 — the emotional payoff) → gentle guitar settling on the loop close (Frame 6).
- **Texture note:** comedic but warm — never slapstick, never mocking. The humor is affectionate.
- **Loop:** clean 12s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT B-5 — "Confidence Is Contagious"

- **Feeling:** empowerment / hype
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a bold high-volume blowout, face-framing curtain bangs, glossy jet-black, bouncy and full
- **Magic move:** as she walks down a street feeling herself, **the whole city dresses up around her** — buildings gain neon trim, puddles become mirrors, streetlights bloom into chandeliers, grey pedestrians gain color — her energy infects everything
- **Concept line:** "I didn't change the city — the city changed for me"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken tracking shot down an evening city sidewalk, 7 frames
- **Loop:** final frame returns the street to its neutral grey pre-walk state

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | center of screen | 8 feet from camera | front pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`, full body visible head-to-feet, positioned **dead center of screen**, approximately **8 feet from lens**. She steps out of a taxi, one foot on the curb, straightening up, one hand adjusting her collar — the first moment of arrival.

- **Wardrobe:** a long structured black wool coat, belted at the waist, over a fitted deep-red silk blouse with a high mandarin collar, black tailored cigarette pants.

- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** slim rectangular matte-black sunglasses (pushed slightly down the nose so eyes are visible above); a bold gold statement ring on the index finger; thin gold ear-climbers; a black structured clutch under the arm; deep cherry glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front, **dead center**, one foot on the curb, weight shifting upward — the arrival stance.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **8 feet back**, shooting her head-on.
- **Background (powerful):** an evening city street that's currently **neutral and grey** — concrete buildings, a few dim streetlights, puddles from recent rain reflecting dull grey, ordinary pedestrians in muted clothing passing. Nothing special. The taxi pulls away behind her.
- **Lighting:** flat grey evening ambient; a single weak streetlight overhead; the taxi taillights fading red behind her.
- **Color & Vibrance:** deliberately muted/neutral — grey sidewalk, grey buildings, dim lights — setting up the contrast. Only her deep-red blouse and cherry nails read as saturated (she's the only color source).
- **Composition:** Aira dead center, the grey street receding behind her, she is the only vivid element.
- **Facial Expression:** cool composure settling into confidence — chin lifting, eyes steady above the sunglasses, lips in a controlled almost-smile, brow smooth. She's about to own this street and she knows it.
- **Object Interaction:** one hand adjusts the coat collar with precision (fingertip-on-fabric contact, straightening the mandarin collar beneath); the clutch is pinned under the other arm with natural pressure.

- **Lighting Behavior:** flat and grey — but the faint warm glow begins at her feet as she steps forward (barely noticeable).
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus, everything legible, nothing special yet.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — B-5 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** a building cinematic power-groove — starts stripped and cool, grows into a full orchestral-electronic triumphant walk-track. The "main character just arrived" anthem.
- **Tempo / key:** ~105 BPM, D minor (power), driving and relentless but glossy.

- **Arc:** sub-bass pulse only (Frame 1 — grey) → snare + first synth layer on the neon growth (Frame 2) → full build at the close-up (Frame 3) → the bass-drop + full orchestral hit at the city-wake frame (Frame 4 — the hero moment) → solo piano over the sub on the glance-back (Frame 5 — intimate) → strip to sub-bass only on the loop (Frame 6).
- **Texture note:** this needs to feel like a movie trailer when the city transforms — cinematic, building, powerful — but drop to intimate on the glance-back for contrast.
- **Loop:** clean 12s loop matching the visual loop point.
