## CONCEPT C-1 — "The Locket Opens"

- **Feeling:** curiosity / hook (series-building)
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** loose romantic side-swept waves, all hair over one shoulder, deep amber-honey tone, ends brushing the waist
- **Magic move:** a vintage gold locket opens and releases a **miniature living world** — tiny glowing butterflies, a pocket-sized aurora, a microscopic garden — that expands into the air around her before being gently pulled back inside when she closes it
- **Concept line:** "what's inside changes every time"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move in a twilight rooftop garden, 7 frames
- **Loop:** the locket snaps closed and resets to its resting position, ready to open again

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | left third of screen | 8 feet from camera | front pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body visible head-to-feet, positioned in the **left third of screen**, approximately **8 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** loose romantic side-swept waves, all hair swept over the left shoulder, deep amber-honey tone, ends brushing the waist.
- **Wardrobe:** a flowing dusty-lavender silk maxi dress with a deep V-neckline and thin straps, soft gathered waist, the skirt catching a rooftop breeze.
- **Footwear:** delicate gold strappy flat sandals, thin ankle wraps visible, relaxed stance.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** a vintage gold oval locket on a long fine chain resting at her sternum (THE recurring object); thin gold rings, small gold ear-studs, soft mauve glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front pose with slight hip-shift right, head tilted softly left, one hand resting at her collarbone near the locket.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **8 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a lush twilight rooftop garden — climbing jasmine on wrought-iron trellises, terracotta pots overflowing with deep-purple and magenta bougainvillea, string of warm Edison bulbs, a weathered stone balustrade, and beyond it a vast twilight city skyline glowing amber-blue. A deep violet-to-peach gradient sky.
- **Lighting:** warm Edison-bulb practicals as key (multiple soft points); cool twilight ambient; a soft golden rim from the last sliver of sun on the horizon behind the skyline.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — C-1 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** ethereal cinematic wonder — delicate, curious, magical but not whimsical/childish. Think a music-box melody grown up and given an orchestra.
- **Tempo / key:** ~72 BPM, E major (bright, open), gentle and unhurried.
- **Core elements:** a delicate celeste/music-box motif (the "locket theme" — 4 notes that recur every episode); a warm cello underpinning; soft finger-picked harp; a breathy pad that swells with the magic; tiny bell accents for the butterflies.
- **Arc:** celeste motif alone on Frame 1 (curiosity) → harp and cello enter as the locket opens (Frame 2) → full swell with pad as the swarm expands (Frames 3–4) → the motif returns gently as the magic recalls (Frame 5) → single celeste + cello on the hook-look (Frame 6) → bare motif on the loop close (Frame 7).
- **Texture note:** the 4-note celeste motif MUST be distinctive and memorable — it's the recurring "locket" sonic brand for the series.
- **Loop:** clean 14s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT C-2 — "The Vintage Key"

- **Feeling:** curiosity / intrigue (series-building)
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a sleek center-part low ponytail, incredibly long, tied with a thin leather cord, razor-straight, ink-black
- **Magic move:** an ornate skeleton key turns in mid-air (no door) and a **portal of living light** cracks open — a sliver of another world visible through it (a sun-drenched Mediterranean coast), wind and warmth blasting through, before she turns the key back and it seals
- **Concept line:** "the key fits everywhere and nowhere"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move in a moody industrial loft at night, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the key settles back into her palm, the air heals, the loft returns to silent still

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | right third of screen | 7 feet from camera | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body visible head-to-feet, positioned in the **right third of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** sleek center-part low ponytail, razor-straight, ink-black, incredibly long (past the waist), tied with a thin brown leather cord.
- **Wardrobe:** a fitted black ribbed turtleneck tucked into high-waist wide-leg dark-olive cargo trousers, a wide brown leather belt with an aged brass buckle.
- **Footwear:** chunky black leather combat boots, worn-in, with brass buckle detailing.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** no eyewear; a single thick silver thumb-ring, small silver hoop earrings, an ornate vintage skeleton key (THE recurring object) held loosely in her right hand at her side — aged brass, intricate teeth, a small loop at the bow; deep espresso glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, three-quarter pose facing slightly left, weight settled, one hand at her side holding the key loosely between thumb and forefinger.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **7 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a vast industrial loft at night — exposed steel beams, tall steel-frame windows showing a dark rain-streaked city, polished concrete floor, a single bare-filament Edison bulb hanging on a long cord as the only light source, raw brick walls, sparse — one worn leather armchair, stacked old books. Moody, minimal, powerful.
- **Lighting:** single bare Edison bulb as key (harsh warm pool, sharp shadows); cool blue city-rain light from the windows; the rest deep shadow.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated warm Edison gold in the pool + cool blue rain-light + deep olive trousers + the aged brass key as the warm accent — moody but vivid where the light touches. Rich blacks.
- **Composition:** Aira right third in the Edison pool, the vast dark loft receding left, the empty air center-left where the portal will appear.
- **Facial Expression:** focused intention — eyes level and slightly narrowed, brow set with quiet determination, lips pressed in a thin decisive line, jaw set. She knows what the key does. She's deciding.
- **Object Interaction:** the key hangs between her right thumb and forefinger — a casual but deliberate grip, the weight of the brass palpable, her fingers making real contact with the aged metal.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 static hold at 7 feet — building tension in the stillness.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she breathes in, shoulders lifting; 0:01–0:02 she raises the key to the air in front of her — a slow, deliberate lift.
- **Object Action:** the Edison bulb sways faintly; rain streaks the windows; the key catches the light as it rises.
- **Physics:** the key has correct brass weight — it doesn't float up, she lifts it with real arm-effort; the bulb sways with building vibration; rain on glass has correct streak-speed.
- **Object Interaction:** her grip on the key stays precise through the lift — thumb and forefinger controlling the rotation so the teeth face forward.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 determination holding; 0:01 eyes narrow further — decision made; 0:02 a single decisive exhale, lips parting.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the Edison pool stays fixed; the key's brass catches and throws a small warm glint as it rises into the light.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus, still and tense.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the rain on windows (steady, atmospheric); a single distant thunder-roll; the concrete room-tone (vast, hollow); Edison buzz; the key's metal warming in her hand (a faint tonal hum — the anticipation).
- **Loop note:** key-at-her-side is the master reference.

### FRAME 2 — medium (waist up) | center of screen | 4 feet from camera | front pose | slight low angle

- **Lighting:** the portal-crack as a blazing warm key, blasting golden light onto her face and torso from straight ahead; Edison behind her now secondary.
- **Color & Vibrance:** BLAZING golden portal-light + the turquoise-and-white of the Mediterranean sliver + her dark outfit as contrast — extreme light-vs-dark drama.
- **Composition:** her at center, the key at the exact midpoint of frame, the golden crack splitting the air directly beyond the key — key as the fulcrum.
- **Facial Expression:** the turn has been made — a flash of intensity: eyes wide and lit by the portal-blast, brow up, lips parted, chin lifted against the light. Not fear — exhilaration. The wind from the other world blowing her ponytail back.
- **Object Interaction:** the key is turned 90 degrees in the air (as if in an invisible lock), her grip firm, wrist rotated, the teeth of the key aligned with the crack they've made.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:02–0:04 static low hold — the portal does the work.
- **Subject Action:** 0:02–0:03 she turns the key in the air (a firm wrist rotation); 0:03–0:04 holds the turned position as the crack blasts open.
- **Object Action:** the air CRACKS — a vertical seam of golden light splits open from the key-teeth outward, widening; warm wind blasts through, carrying Mediterranean scent-visuals (a bougainvillea petal, salt mist); the crack widens to a 2-foot-wide portal.
- **Physics:** the crack opens with believable material-tearing physics (like light breaking through); the wind blast has correct directional force (her hair and ponytail blow straight back, turtleneck fabric presses); the petal tumbles with real air-resistance.
- **Object Interaction:** the key stays locked in her firm grip through the turn — wrist rotation is precise; the invisible resistance of the "lock" is felt in her arm tension.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:02 the wrist turns — determination; 0:03 the blast hits — eyes widen, squint against light, mouth opens; 0:04 settling into exhilaration — the squint becomes a fierce grin against the wind.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the golden blast ramps from crack-thin to flooding — her whole face and body progressively illuminated.
- **Lens / Optical:** the light blast creates a natural bloom/flare across the lens; focus holds her face.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the AIR CRACK (a visceral tearing sound — deep, resonant, powerful); the blast of wind (whooshing, warm); ocean sounds from the other world (waves, gulls); a bougainvillea petal passing the mic; her gasp against the wind.
- **Loop note:** —

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — C-2 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** dark cinematic tension into explosive warmth — a building atmospheric thriller-score that BURSTS into warm Mediterranean brightness at the portal, then contracts back.
- **Tempo / key:** starts ~70 BPM in A minor (tense), explodes to ~100 BPM in D major (the portal world), contracts back to 70 BPM in A minor (close).
- **Core elements:** a deep sustained drone and rain-texture for the loft; sharp metallic percussive hits for the key-turn; a full warm acoustic guitar + hand-drum + bouzouki explosion for the Mediterranean blast; then the drone reasserts.
- **Arc:** drone + rain (Frame 1) → metallic hits on the key-turn (Frame 2) → FULL Mediterranean music blasts in simultaneously with the portal (Frames 2–3, like a door opening on a party) → fades as the portal narrows (Frame 4) → the seal "THOOM" kills all music for one beat of silence → drone returns (Frame 5) → settles to the opening texture (Frame 6 loop).
- **Texture note:** the contrast between the dark drone and the bright Mediterranean blast IS the emotional hook. It should feel like stepping from winter into summer in one frame.
- **Loop:** clean 12s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT C-3 — "The Mirror Shows Tomorrow"

- **Feeling:** curiosity / intrigue (series-building)
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a high sleek topknot with a single thick strand wrapped around the base, no flyaways, sculpted and sharp
- **Magic move:** an antique hand-mirror shows NOT her reflection but a **scene from tomorrow** — a glimpse of the next day (her in a different outfit, different location, doing something surprising) — then the image fades
- **Concept line:** "I already know what happens next"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move in a candlelit boudoir at night, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the mirror returns to showing her normal reflection

---

### FRAME 1 — three-quarter body (knees up) | center of screen | 5 feet from camera | front pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.

- **Footwear:** black satin pointed-toe mules with a small kitten heel.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** an ornate antique oval hand-mirror (THE recurring object) — gilded frame, slightly tarnished, held in her right hand resting face-up on her lap; a thin velvet choker with a tiny ruby pendant; deep wine glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter body (knees up), front, **center**, seated at the edge of a chaise longue, mirror resting face-up in her lap.
- **Camera:** eye-level (at her seated height), 40mm, **5 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** a romantic candlelit boudoir — a deep-emerald velvet chaise, heavy brocade curtains, a tall ornate gilded floor-mirror (showing nothing yet), dozens of ivory candles of varying heights on brass candelabras, dried dark roses, a Persian rug — opulent, moody, flame-lit.
- **Lighting:** warm flickering candlelight from multiple points; no electric light; deep dancing shadows; the mirror catching and bouncing one candle-point.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated burgundy + emerald + gold gilt + ivory candle + wine nails — rich, dark, romantic palette.
- **Composition:** Aira center on the chaise, the candles framing her, the hand-mirror in her lap as the quiet focal pull.
- **Facial Expression:** contemplative curiosity — eyes lowered to the mirror in her lap, brow in soft thought, lips relaxed with a faint interested curve, chin tilted down. About to look.
- **Object Interaction:** the mirror rests face-up on her thigh, her right hand holding the gilded handle, left hand resting beside it — about to lift it.

- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 slow push-in from 5 to 4 feet, gentle and intimate.

- **Object Action:** candle flames dance; the mirror surface catches light as it tilts; the room holds its breath.
- **Physics:** the mirror has correct gilded-metal weight (she lifts with real effort through the wrist); candle flames respond to the micro-air current of her arm moving; velvet dress shifts with the lift motion.
- **Object Interaction:** her grip on the ornate handle is precise — fingers wrapping the contours, the tarnished gold meeting skin with real contact.

- **Lighting Behavior:** as the mirror tilts, it catches a candle point and throws a small golden light-sweep across the ceiling.
- **Lens / Optical:** focus eases from medium to slightly shallow as the push-in lands.
- **Diegetic Sound:** candle-wax drip; fabric shift of velvet; the mirror lifting (a soft weighted metallic sound); her inhale; crackling flame.
- **Loop note:** mirror-in-lap state is the master reference.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — C-3 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** intimate dark-romantic mystery — a boudoir-noir soundtrack. Candlelit, knowing, sensual but not overt.
- **Tempo / key:** ~65 BPM, D minor, slow and deliberate.
- **Core elements:** a solo cello playing a languid theme; soft finger-picked classical guitar; a low sustained pad; candle-crackle texture woven in; a brief bright acoustic motif (the tomorrow-theme) that plays only during the mirror-vision and disappears when it fades.
- **Arc:** cello solo (Frame 1) → the tomorrow-theme bursts in bright during the mirror-vision (Frame 2, contrasting) → fades as the vision dissolves (Frame 3) → cello + guitar settle (Frame 4 hook) → returns to solo cello (Frame 5 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the tomorrow-theme must sound like it belongs to a DIFFERENT genre (light, bright, acoustic morning music) — the contrast between the dark boudoir and the bright tomorrow is the whole magic.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT C-4 — "The Music Box Dances"

- **Feeling:** wonder / tenderness (series-building)
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** soft cascading ringlet curls, honey-gold, shoulder-length, a single pearl clip holding one side back
- **Magic move:** an antique music box opens and its tiny ballerina figurine steps OFF the mechanism, grows to life-size, and dances one perfect pirouette beside Aira — then shrinks back down and returns to the box
- **Concept line:** "she only dances when I wind her up"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move in a soft-lit bedroom at golden hour, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the music box closes and the figurine is back in place, frozen, ready to wind again

---

## CONCEPT C-5 — "The Snow Globe Shakes Itself"

- **Feeling:** cozy magic / curiosity (series-building)
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a thick loose fishtail braid draped over one shoulder, dark espresso-brown, ends tied with a thin gold thread
- **Magic move:** a large antique snow globe on a shelf SHAKES ITSELF (nobody touches it) and the scene inside comes alive — miniature snow falls inside, tiny lights ignite in the tiny buildings, and the same snow begins drifting into the REAL room through the glass
- **Concept line:** "it starts on its own when the time is right"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move in a cozy cabin at evening, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the snow settles, the globe stills, the room returns to normal

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | right third of screen | 7 feet from camera | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **right third of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** thick loose fishtail braid over the right shoulder, dark espresso-brown, gold thread at the end.
- **Wardrobe:** an oversized oatmeal cable-knit sweater dress reaching mid-thigh, chunky and cozy, a thin brown leather belt at the waist.
- **Footwear:** thick cream wool socks (no shoes), padding on a dark wood floor.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** the antique snow globe (THE recurring object) on a high shelf behind her — large, brass-based, containing a tiny alpine village; small gold stud earrings, a simple gold band ring, warm nude glossy nails; a mug of hot cocoa in her hands.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, three-quarter pose, **right third**, standing mid-room with the cocoa, the globe visible on the shelf behind her upper-left.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **7 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a cozy mountain cabin at evening — dark wood walls, a crackling stone fireplace with amber flames, thick knit throws on a deep leather armchair, tall bookshelves, frosted windows showing a dark snowy night outside, warm lighting. The antique snow globe sits on a high shelf, prominent.
- **Lighting:** warm fireplace key (flickering amber); soft lamp fill; the frosted window casting cool blue rim; the globe catching a shelf-lamp spotlight.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated warm amber + oatmeal + dark wood + cool blue window + the globe's tiny internal warm glow — cozy, rich, hygge but vivid.
- **Composition:** Aira right third with cocoa, the snow globe upper-left on the shelf (the eye travels to it), fireplace filling center-right behind her.
- **Facial Expression:** cozy contentment — eyes soft and unfocused (thinking/daydreaming), a gentle warm smile behind the mug she's about to sip, brow relaxed, completely at peace.
- **Object Interaction:** both hands wrap the mug (white ceramic, cocoa steam rising) — a heat-seeking grip, knuckles defined, warmth-transfer visible.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 static hold at 7 feet — cozy stillness.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she lifts the mug for a slow sip, eyes closing; 0:01–0:02 lowers the mug, eyes reopening to a sound behind her — the globe.
- **Object Action:** 0:01 — the snow globe on the shelf begins to VIBRATE on its own. A faint rattle. Then it SHAKES — a contained, gentle wobble — and inside, snow begins to swirl.
- **Physics:** the globe vibrates with correct mass-on-shelf physics (a heavy brass object wobbling); the internal snow swirls with realistic water-globe physics; her braid sways as she turns.
- **Object Interaction:** she doesn't touch the globe — it moves alone. Her mug lowers with correct ceramic weight.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 contentment, eyes closing for the sip; 0:01 eyes open to the sound — surprise, brow up, mouth leaving the mug; 0:02 curious intrigue — she turns her head toward the shelf.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the globe's internal tiny lights ignite — warm pinpoints visible on the shelf.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — both her and the globe legible.
- **Diegetic Sound:** fireplace crackle; cocoa sip; the globe's rattle-vibrate (soft brass-on-wood); the internal snow-swirl (a muffled whoosh); her surprised "hmm?"; the tiny lights igniting (soft chime).
- **Loop note:** globe-still-on-shelf is the master reference.

### FRAME 3 — full body | center of screen | 6 feet from camera | front pose | slight low angle (HERO)
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`

- **Lighting:** the globe's light + fireplace amber + each snowflake as a tiny golden light-point = a room full of floating warm stars.
- **Color & Vibrance:** MAXIMUM cozy magic — warm amber + white snow + oatmeal + the golden flake-glints — like being inside a living snow globe yourself.
- **Composition:** Aira center, snow falling all around her, fireplace behind, the glowing globe above-left on the shelf — she IS inside the snow globe now.

- **Object Interaction:** arms slightly open, palms up, catching snowflakes — an offering/receiving pose. Snow lands on her palms, shoulders, braid.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:04–0:06 slow crane-down to the low angle, holding — the hero shot.
- **Subject Action:** 0:04–0:05 she opens her arms and tilts her face up; 0:05–0:06 a slow spin on the spot (quarter-turn), eyes closed, bathing in it.
- **Object Action:** the snowfall is at full intensity — filling the room, dusting every surface, the fire somehow coexisting, the globe pulsing with light.
- **Physics:** snow obeys correct drift-speed and accumulation; her spin creates a micro-vortex that swirls nearby flakes; the fire's heat creates a snow-free bubble directly above it (realistic convection); her braid lifts with the spin.
- **Object Interaction:** snow lands on her continuously — palms, shoulders, lashes, braid — with correct tiny-weight contact.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:04 eyes closing, smile growing; 0:05 full bliss during the spin; 0:06 a joyful laugh-exhale, catching a flake on her tongue.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the low angle makes the snowfall read as a canopy of golden stars above her.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — the whole snow-room is the spectacle.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the full indoor snowfall (a soft crystalline ambient — like being inside gentle static); the fireplace still crackling; the globe humming; her joyful laugh; the tiny patter of snow accumulating; wind-chime quality to the flakes.
- **Loop note:** —

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — C-5 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** cozy cinematic warmth with a magical shimmer — a winter-evening score. Hygge-meets-Narnia.
- **Tempo / key:** ~68 BPM, Eb major, gentle and enveloping.
- **Core elements:** a soft solo piano motif (the "globe theme" — simple, cozy, 6 notes); warm low strings; a celeste/glockenspiel shimmer for the snowfall; sleigh-bell texture (very subtle, not cheesy); a crackling-fire texture woven in.
- **Arc:** solo piano + fire-crackle (Frame 1) → the globe-shake gets a low rumble + celeste entering (Frame 2) → full strings + glockenspiel shimmer at the indoor snowfall hero (Frame 3 — emotional peak) → thins to solo piano + celeste as snow recedes (Frame 4) → returns to solo piano + fire (Frame 5 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the celeste/glockenspiel IS the snow — it enters with the flakes and leaves with them. The piano is the cabin. They coexist.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

# IDEA D — "SHOW THE FEELING"
*Feeling: oddly satisfying / want. Make an invisible sensation visible around Aira — pure mood, no product. The kind of reel people send to a friend saying "this is such a vibe."*

## CONCEPT D-1 — "The First Sip of Cold Water on a Hot Day"

- **Feeling:** oddly satisfying / visceral relief
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a high messy textured ponytail, sun-bleached caramel-brown, wispy face-framing pieces, effortless summer
- **Magic move:** the moment she sips cold water, a wave of visible BLUE CHILL radiates outward from her body — frost-crystals bloom on the glass she's holding, her breath becomes visible for one frame, and every surface near her frosts momentarily — then it all melts back in seconds
- **Concept line:** "that first sip hit different"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move on a sun-blazing rooftop terrace, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the frost melts, the heat returns, she reaches for the glass again

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | center of screen | 7 feet from camera | front pose | slight low angle
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** high messy textured ponytail, sun-bleached caramel-brown, wispy face-framing pieces, effortless.
- **Wardrobe:** a white linen cropped button-up tied at the waist, high-waist terracotta linen wide-leg pants, relaxed and breezy.
- **Footwear:** brown leather flat slide sandals, toes relaxed, one ankle crossed.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** round tortoise-shell sunglasses pushed up on the head; a stack of thin gold bangles; small gold hoops; a tall glass of ice water with condensation dripping on a terrace table beside her; soft peach glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front, **center**, leaning on the terrace railing, one elbow on the rail, the water glass on the table beside her.
- **Camera:** slight low angle (hip height), 35mm, deep focus, **7 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a sun-blazing Mediterranean rooftop terrace — white-washed walls, terracotta tiles, a vivid bougainvillea cascade (hot pink), a turquoise sea visible beyond the railing, harsh midday sun overhead, heat-shimmer visible on the tiles. HOT. Everything radiates summer heat.
- **Lighting:** harsh overhead midday sun (strong top-key, short shadows); warm bounce off white walls; the heat itself visible as shimmer in the air.
- **Color & Vibrance:** MAXIMUM summer — white + terracotta + hot-pink bougainvillea + turquoise sea + caramel hair — blazing saturated heat-palette.
- **Composition:** Aira center leaning on the rail, the ice-water glass as the focal object beside her hand, the hot terrace radiating all around.
- **Facial Expression:** heat-discomfort softening into thirst — eyes slightly squinted against the glare, a visible sheen on the skin (not sweating excessively — glowing), lips slightly parted for a breath, brow relaxed but warm. She's about to reach for relief.
- **Object Interaction:** her right hand reaches for the sweating glass — fingertips approaching the cold condensation with obvious anticipation.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 static hold at 7 feet — the heat establishes.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she breathes against the heat (chest rises); 0:01–0:02 she reaches for the glass and wraps her hand around it — a visible micro-shiver of cold.
- **Object Action:** the glass sweats; condensation drips; ice clinks; the heat-shimmer waves above the tiles; bougainvillea sways in hot breeze.
- **Physics:** the heat-shimmer is correct convection distortion; condensation drips with water-gravity; ice settles with correct clinky physics; her wispy hair lifts in the hot breeze.
- **Object Interaction:** her hand wraps the glass — fingertips meeting the wet cold surface, a visible flinch-then-grip of relief; condensation wets her fingers.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 heat-squint; 0:01 the reach — thirst, anticipation; 0:02 the grip — a micro-relief, eyes softening, lips pressing together in a pre-sip settle.
- **Lighting Behavior:** harsh and hot, steady — about to be disrupted.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus, the heat-shimmer creating natural distortion in the air.
- **Diegetic Sound:** cicadas LOUD; the hot breeze; ice clinking in the glass; distant sea; her heat-breath; the glass condensation dripping onto hot tile (a sizzle-hiss).
- **Loop note:** glass-on-table / heat-state is the master reference.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:02–0:04 static intimate hold — the sip is the event.
- **Subject Action:** 0:02–0:03 the glass tilts, she sips — slow, deliberate, savoring; 0:03–0:04 she lowers the glass and — THE CHILL HITS.
- **Object Action:** the MOMENT the water touches her lips: a visible wave of BLUE-WHITE CHILL radiates outward from her body in all directions. Frost-crystals BLOOM explosively on the glass surface. Her breath becomes visible (cold vapor). The nearest terracotta tile frosts white. The bougainvillea leaves nearest her frost at the edges.
- **Physics:** the frost-bloom follows real ice-crystal formation patterns (dendritic, branching); the chill-wave travels at a visible speed (fast but trackable — like a shockwave); breath-vapor forms correctly in the sudden local cold; the frost on the tile follows the grout lines.
- **Object Interaction:** the glass frosts in her grip — her wet fingers leave clear unfrosted prints where skin contacts glass (detail!); the glass weight doesn't change.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:02 the anticipatory close; 0:03 THE SIP — and the RELIEF: eyes fly open wide, brow shoots up, mouth releases the glass with a sharp satisfied exhale; 0:04 eyes rolling back slightly in pure ecstasy, a slow "mmm" expression forming — bliss.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the chill-wave carries a brief cool-blue light-shift that washes over her face and the frame, then fades — a momentary color temperature drop.
- **Lens / Optical:** the chill-wave creates a brief refractive distortion in the air (like heat-shimmer but inverted — a cold-shimmer).
- **Diegetic Sound:** the sip (a cold-water gulp); THE CHILL: a deep satisfying bass-drop "WHOOOMPH" (felt in the chest) + a crystalline frost-crackle spreading rapidly + the breath-vapor (a sharp cold exhale); cicadas cutting to silence for one beat; then returning.
- **Loop note:** —

- **Camera:** slight low angle (hip height), 28mm, **6 feet from lens**, heroic.
- **Background (powerful):** the ENTIRE hot terrace momentarily frosted — tiles white, bougainvillea ice-edged, railing crystalized, the sea still turquoise beyond (the frost only reaches so far) — a winter moment frozen into summer. Steam rises from where frost meets hot surfaces.
- **Lighting:** the light has shifted briefly to cool-blue key (the sun filtered through the chill-wave); frost surfaces catching and refracting light into prismatic sparkle.
- **Color & Vibrance:** INVERTED PALETTE — cool blue-white frost over the hot terracotta/pink/turquoise, creating a startling contrast. Her warm skin tone is the only warm element.
- **Composition:** Aira center in the frosted world, her warm skin the focal heat-point, frost radiating out from her in all directions, the unfrosted turquoise sea as the horizon.
- **Facial Expression:** pure cold-water ECSTASY — head tilted back, eyes closed, mouth in a slow satisfied "ahhh" shape, every feature relaxed in complete relief. The universal "that hit" face.
- **Object Interaction:** the frosted glass held slightly raised (a toast to herself), her wet-cold fingers leaving prints, ice still clinking inside.

**VIDEO PROMPT**

- **Object Action:** the frost is at PEAK — everything white and crystalline; then: it begins to MELT. Fast. Steam rises from every surface as the summer heat fights back. Drips form. The frost recedes outward from her (her body-heat is the first thing to unfreeze things).
- **Physics:** frost melts with correct water-state transition — first thin, then wet, then dripping; steam rises from hot surfaces reclaiming the frost; melting follows heat-source logic (things nearest the sun melt first); the prismatic sparkle fades with the ice.
- **Object Interaction:** the glass in her raised hand defrosts — condensation returning to normal dripping; her grip adjusts.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:04 full head-back ecstasy; 0:05 the "ahhh" — mouth open, brow up, total relief; 0:06 a slow returning — head lowering, eyes opening, a broad satisfied grin.
- **Lighting Behavior:** cool-blue shifting back to hot gold as the frost melts — the color temperature rising in real time.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus reads the whole frosted-then-melting scene.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the frost crackling as it melts (a cascade of tiny ice-breaking sounds); steam hissing off hot tiles; dripping water; the cicadas rushing back in; her satisfied "ahhh" exhale; the summer reclaiming.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — D-1 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** hot summer minimalism with a satisfying bass-drop payoff — Balearic chill meets cinematic impact.
- **Tempo / key:** ~95 BPM, D major (warm), airy and spacious.
- **Core elements:** a lazy summer guitar-loop (clean, muted, rhythmic); a warm sub-bass pad; cicada-texture woven in; and at the CHILL moment: a MASSIVE satisfying sub-bass DROP + a crystalline reverse-cymbal + frozen silence for one beat — the musical equivalent of "ahhh."
- **Arc:** lazy guitar + cicada (Frame 1 — hot) → building anticipation (strip to sub-bass only at the sip) → THE DROP at the chill-wave (Frame 2–3, the payoff, deeply satisfying) → the guitar returns warm as summer reclaims (Frame 4) → settles to the opening lazy loop (Frame 5 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the DROP must be DEEPLY SATISFYING — like the audio equivalent of cracking your back. The whole track builds to that one moment of cold-relief.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT D-2 — "The Feeling When Your Song Comes On"

- **Feeling:** euphoria / the body-takeover moment
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** space buns (two high symmetrical buns), sleek and glossy black, with two thin face-framing tendrils
- **Magic move:** the instant a beat drops in her headphones, visible SOUNDWAVES ripple outward from her ears in concentric rings — colors pulse with the bass, her hair and clothes move with the rhythm as if underwater, and the entire room's colors SHIFT with each beat
- **Concept line:** "when the song finds you"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move in a minimalist white studio that becomes a living equalizer, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the song ends, color drains, everything stills — then the first beat hits again

---

### FRAME 1 — three-quarter body (knees up) | left third of screen | 5 feet from camera | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Three-quarter body (knees up), positioned **left third of screen**, approximately **5 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** space buns (two high symmetrical buns), sleek glossy black, two thin face-framing tendrils.
- **Wardrobe:** a fitted black ribbed tank-top, oversized low-slung white cargo jeans with black stitching, a cropped black leather jacket slung over one shoulder.
- **Footwear:** chunky white platform sneakers with black accents.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** oversized black over-ear headphones (THE key prop) around her neck (not on ears yet); a chain necklace with a small lightning-bolt pendant; black matte nails; two thin silver rings.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter body (knees up), 3/4 pose, **left third**, standing in the center of a white room, jacket slung casually, one hand reaching for the headphones.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 40mm, **5 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** a stark minimalist white studio — white walls, white floor, white ceiling, no furniture, no distractions. Clinical. Empty. The "before" space that the music will transform. One wall has a faint grid of thin grey lines (like graph paper — this will become the equalizer).
- **Lighting:** flat, even white studio lighting — bright, clinical, no shadow, no warmth. Deliberately bland.
- **Color & Vibrance:** deliberately FLAT — white, grey, black only (her outfit is the only dark element). No color. Setting up the contrast.
- **Composition:** Aira left third in the white void, the grid-wall behind her, emptiness everywhere — waiting to be filled.
- **Facial Expression:** anticipatory focus — eyes slightly narrowed in concentration, one side of her lip bitten, brow set. She's choosing a song. The moment before the moment.
- **Object Interaction:** her right hand lifts the headphones from her neck, about to place them over her ears — fingers hooked under the headband.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 static hold — the emptiness establishes.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she lifts the headphones; 0:01–0:02 places them over her ears with both hands, settling them — a ritual.
- **Object Action:** the white room waits; the grid lines are static; nothing happens yet.
- **Physics:** headphones have correct weight and cushion-compression as they settle; the jacket slung on her shoulder has correct leather weight.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — D-2 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** THIS IS THE ACTUAL SONG SHE'S LISTENING TO — a custom beat that builds from silence to an explosive euphoric drop. Think Flume meets Disclosure — electronic, bass-heavy, euphoric.
- **Tempo / key:** ~128 BPM, F minor, four-on-floor with heavy sub-bass.
- **Core elements:** builds from a single distant synth-note → layered with a driving hat pattern → a pitched vocal chop → then THE DROP: full sub-bass, punchy kick, euphoric synth-lead, layered vocal chops — maximum energy → strip-back to the opening single note.
- **Arc:** single note + silence (Frame 1) → the build begins (0:01–0:02) → THE DROP at Frame 2 (0:02, full impact) → rides at full energy through Frame 3 (hero) → begins to fade/filter-sweep down through Frame 4 → strip to single note on Frame 5 (loop close).
- **Texture note:** the DROP must hit HARD — like walking into a club at the perfect moment. The contrast between the silent white room and the full beat is the whole experience.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT D-3 — "The Smell of Rain on Hot Pavement"

- **Feeling:** nostalgia / sensory longing
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** long loose natural waves, dark chocolate-brown, middle part, air-dried texture, reaching mid-back
- **Magic move:** the first raindrop hits the hot ground beside her and the SMELL becomes visible — golden-amber particulate clouds rise from the pavement like spirits, swirling around her, she breathes them in and they glow brighter inside her silhouette for a moment
- **Concept line:** "petrichor never lies"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move on a city sidewalk as a summer storm breaks, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the rain stops, pavement dries, she waits for the next drop

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | right third of screen | 7 feet from camera | three-quarter pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`

Tension in the air.

- **Object Interaction:** the raindrop hits her palm with a real tiny splash-contact; the sandals swing from her flinch.

- **Background (powerful):** the sidewalk returned to hot-and-dry (summer storms pass fast), heat-shimmer returning, storm-clouds reforming on the horizon. Another storm coming.
- **Lighting:** identical amber-grey pre-storm light returning.
- **Color & Vibrance:** matched storm-drama palette.
- **Composition:** identical to Frame 1 for seamless loop.
- **Facial Expression:** sensory anticipation — eyes closed, face up, nostrils flared — the exact opening face. Another storm coming.
- **Object Interaction:** sandals dangling, left palm open — the exact opening pose.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:08–0:10 eases back to the opening composition at 7 feet.
- **Subject Action:** 0:08–0:09 she tilts her face up again; 0:09–0:10 nostrils flare — she smells the next one coming.
- **Object Action:** heat-shimmer returning; new storm-clouds darkening; the air going electric again.
- **Physics:** all matched to opening.
- **Object Interaction:** sandals dangle, palm open — matched.

- **Loop note:** **LOOP POINT** — positions, light, state, and expression match Frame 1 exactly.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — D-3 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** organic ambient with a visceral bass-impact — nature's ASMR meets cinematic emotion. Petrichor as a genre.
- **Tempo / key:** ~75 BPM, A minor (yearning), slow and spacious.
- **Core elements:** recorded rain textures (light to heavy, real recordings); a deep sub-bass "bloom" at the petrichor moment; a warm analog synth-pad that swells with the golden glow; sparse piano notes (3-4, placed, not a melody — like memories); thunder-rumble as percussion.
- **Arc:** sparse piano + distant thunder (Frame 1 — anticipation) → the sub-bass BLOOM + golden pad at the first drop/petrichor moment (Frame 2) → FULL rain texture + pad + sub at the hero (Frame 3 — immersive, like being inside the rain) → rain thinning, pad fading, piano returning (Frame 4) → sparse piano alone (Frame 5 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the rain texture must be IMMERSIVE and REAL — like the listener is standing in it. The sub-bass bloom should feel physical — a chest sensation.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT D-4 — "The Moment Before Sleep Takes You"

- **Feeling:** ASMR / hypnotic comfort
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** loose bedtime hair, soft natural black, spread on a white pillow, no tie, face-framing pieces falling naturally
- **Magic move:** as her eyes get heavy, the room around her slowly DISSOLVES into soft clouds — furniture fading, ceiling opening to a gentle starfield, gravity loosening as she and the bedding begin to float imperceptibly upward — the threshold between wake and sleep made visible
- **Concept line:** "the world lets go before you do"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken vertical drift from a bed upward into dissolving space, 6 frames
- **Loop:** she settles back onto the solid bed, room re-forms, eyes flutter open — the threshold resets

---

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — D-4 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** ambient sleep-music that crosses into cinematic void — ASMR meets Interstellar.
- **Tempo / key:** no tempo (free/floating), hovering around Eb major (warm, sleepy).
- **Core elements:** a single held warm synth-pad (like breathing); very sparse piano (one note every 4-5 seconds); a sub-bass that enters and grows as the dreamspace opens; a vast reverb-space that grows from bedroom-intimate to cosmic-infinite; the faintest high-frequency "stars" shimmer.
- **Arc:** intimate piano + pad (Frame 1 — bedroom) → piano fading, pad growing vast, sub entering (Frame 2 — dissolution) → pure sub-bass + cosmic shimmer + breath in infinite reverb (Frame 3 hero — the void) → sub receding, piano notes returning (Frame 4 — return) → intimate piano + pad settled (Frame 5 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the transition from intimate to vast MUST feel physical — the reverb-space widening should make the listener feel the room disappear.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT D-5 — "That Feeling When You Finally Get Home"

- **Feeling:** relief / sanctuary / "I'm safe now"
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a slightly disheveled low ponytail, medium brown, the kind that's been up all day and is about to come down
- **Magic move:** the instant she closes her apartment door behind her, a visible WAVE OF WARMTH radiates from the door outward through the apartment — every surface the wave touches transforms: cold blue light becomes warm amber, sharp angles soften, rigid furniture seems to exhale and settle, and the air itself fills with visible golden motes of comfort
- **Concept line:** "home knew I was coming"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken move from door-closing inward through an apartment transforming, 6 frames
- **Loop:** she opens the door to leave again — the warmth drains, everything goes cold-blue and rigid, ready for the return

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | center of screen | 7 feet from camera | back pose | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet FROM BEHIND, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens** (camera is inside the apartment looking at her back as she faces the closing door).
- **Hairstyle:** slightly disheveled low ponytail, medium brown, seen from behind, a few escaped strands at the nape.
- **Wardrobe:** a charcoal wool coat (work-day coat), still on, a structured bag slung over one shoulder, slightly rumpled from the day.
- **Footwear:** black pointed-toe ankle boots, one heel slightly lifted as if mid-exhale, a faint scuff from the day.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** the bag (structured black leather, minimal) on one shoulder; a simple watch visible at the wrist; no other jewelry visible from behind.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, BACK pose, **center**, facing the just-closed door, one hand still on the brass doorknob, weight sagging back slightly — the "I made it" lean.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **7 feet back** (from inside the apartment looking toward the door).
- **Background (powerful):** her apartment — but currently COLD and UNWELCOMING: cool blue-grey light (no warm lamps on yet), sharp geometric furniture looking rigid, a grey couch looking hard, the air feeling empty and still. The "apartment before you arrive" state.
- **Lighting:** cold blue-grey ambient from uncovered windows (city evening light); no warm sources yet; clinical and lonely.
- **Color & Vibrance:** deliberately cold — blue-grey, charcoal, steel — her charcoal coat blending into the cold apartment. No warmth anywhere.
- **Composition:** her back center, the cold apartment receding behind the camera, the door as her anchor, the brass knob as the trigger-point.
- **Facial Expression:** (from behind — posture is the expression: shoulders DROPPING, spine sagging from its held-up-all-day position, the head tipping forward, the weight releasing backward against the door. Relief in the body.)
- **Object Interaction:** her right hand still on the brass doorknob — the last connection to "outside." Her left shoulder lets the bag start to slide.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 static hold — letting the relief land.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she pushes the door fully shut (the CLICK); 0:01–0:02 her shoulders drop, she sags against the door, head tipping back.
- **Object Action:** THE CLICK — and from the door, a visible WAVE OF WARMTH radiates outward: a shimmering amber pulse that travels across the floor, up the walls, over every surface. Where it passes: blue-grey light BECOMES warm amber; sharp furniture-edges soften slightly; the rigid couch seems to exhale (cushions puffing); golden motes begin appearing in the air.
- **Physics:** the warmth-wave travels at a visible but fast speed (1-2 seconds to fill the room); color-temperature shifts smoothly on every surface; the couch-puff is subtle but real (like a sigh); golden motes drift with correct Brownian motion.
- **Object Interaction:** her hand releases the knob AFTER the click — the warmth-wave triggers from the closure; the bag begins sliding off her shoulder with gravity.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** (from behind — body expression: 0:00 rigid, held; 0:01 the click — instant shoulder-drop; 0:02 full sag, head back, the exhale visible as her whole back releases.)
- **Lighting Behavior:** the warmth-wave transforms the light — cold blue-grey to warm amber sweeping from the door outward, reaching the far wall by 0:02.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — the wave's progression across the apartment readable.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the door CLICK (decisive, satisfying, final); the warmth-wave has a sound (a soft deep "whooom" like a room exhaling + a gentle amber-toned hum); the couch-puff (a tiny fabric exhale); golden motes entering (a quiet sparkle-shimmer); her own exhale — long, deep, total.
- **Loop note:** cold-blue / door-closed-hand-on-knob is the master reference.

A visible transformation from "professional" to "just me." The most relatable face in this set.

- **Physics:** coat falls with real wool-weight; hair cascades with correct released-tension wave; boot-kick has correct leverage and arc; golden mote-puffs where items land.
- **Object Interaction:** the hair-tie release has correct elastic-snap; the coat slides off skin with friction; the boot-kick heel-to-toe lever is precise.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:02 eyes closing — the release; 0:03 the exhale as hair falls (the "ahh" face); 0:04 eyes opening soft and heavy — home.
- **Lighting Behavior:** warm and steady; golden motes puff from the landing coat.
- **Lens / Optical:** medium depth — her and the immediate warm space.

### FRAME 3 — full body | center of screen | 6 feet from camera | front pose | slight low angle (HERO — THE FALL)
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **6 feet from lens**. She's mid-fall backward onto the plush couch — the hero frame.
- **Hairstyle:** hair now FULLY DOWN and FREE, medium brown, mid-air during the fall-back, streaming upward for one gravity-defying frame.
- **Wardrobe:** underneath the coat: a simple fitted black turtleneck and black jeans (the work-underneath), now the only layer.
- **Footwear:** bare feet (boots abandoned), one sock half-off (she didn't even finish — just fell), toes curling.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** thin necklace visible now (a tiny house-shaped pendant — subtle); watch; one sock half-off; natural nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front, **center**, MID-FALL BACKWARD onto the couch — back arched, arms slightly out, hair streaming up, the moment of total surrender to gravity. Caught in the air.
- **Camera:** slight low angle (from coffee-table height), 28mm, **6 feet from lens**, heroic/dramatic.
- **Background (powerful):** the warm apartment with the plush couch directly behind her — ready to catch her; golden motes swirling in the air disturbed by her fall; the candle flame bowing from the air-displacement; cushions about to receive her.
- **Lighting:** full amber warmth; golden motes catching light as they swirl; the candle guttering from her fall-draft.
- **Color & Vibrance:** maximum warm amber + golden motes + the black outfit as grounding contrast — a golden sanctuary.
- **Composition:** her falling form center, arms and hair radiating outward, the couch waiting below, golden motes swirling — the most dynamic frame.
- **Facial Expression:** COMPLETE ABANDON — eyes closed, mouth open in a release-laugh ("ha!"), brow UP (the thrill of the fall), chin lifting, every feature wide-open and FREE. The face of someone who has stopped holding anything up. Gravity is taking over and she LOVES it.
- **Object Interaction:** falling — no grip on anything, arms releasing, body trusting the couch. The half-removed sock dangles from her toes.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:04–0:06 static low hold — the fall plays.
- **Subject Action:** 0:04–0:05 she tips backward (the decision) — arms opening, back arching; 0:05–0:06 she LANDS in the couch (a deep plush impact, cushions swallowing her).
- **Object Action:** the fall displaces air — golden motes WHOOSH outward in a burst; the candle flame BOWS hard; cushions COMPRESS and wrap around her; a throw slides toward her (the couch offering a blanket).
- **Physics:** the fall has correct gravity-acceleration and body-rotation; the landing has real cushion-compression (springs, foam response); the mote-burst follows correct air-displacement patterns; the candle gutters from the draft; the throw slides with fabric-on-fabric friction.
- **Object Interaction:** her body meets the couch with a DEEP satisfying sink — the cushions visibly compressing, her form settling into them, the fabric creasing around her.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:04 the decision face — eyebrows up, grin starting; 0:05 MID-AIR — full abandon laugh; 0:06 the LANDING — eyes-open wide, then closing in bliss as the couch catches her, the laugh becoming a long satisfied "ahhhh."
- **Lighting Behavior:** golden motes swirl in the air-disturbance, creating moving light patterns.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus catching the dynamic motion; air-motes as texture.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the FALL (a whoosh of air); the LANDING (a deep satisfying "FWUMP" of couch-cushion impact — the most satisfying sound in the set); the mote-burst (sparkle-whoosh); the candle guttering; her release-laugh then the satisfied "ahhhh"; the throw fabric sliding.
- **Loop note:** —

- **Object Interaction:** hand on knob — matched.

- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — matched.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — D-5 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** intimate indie-folk warmth with a cinematic swell — the "getting home" anthem. The audio equivalent of a hug.
- **Tempo / key:** ~85 BPM, C major (home key, warm, resolved).
- **Core elements:** a soft fingerpicked acoustic guitar (the home-theme); a warm bass note that enters with the warmth-wave; gentle brushed drums entering at the fall; a warm vocal "ooh" pad (wordless, comforting); returns to solo guitar.
- **Arc:** silence + city-sounds (Frame 1 — cold) → the warmth-wave gets the bass-note entry + guitar beginning (Frame 1 click-moment) → guitar + brushed drums grow through the de-armoring (Frame 2) → FULL arrangement at the couch-fall (Frame 3 — the payoff, warmest) → strips to guitar + vocal pad at the peace (Frame 4) → fades to silence on the loop close (Frame 5).
- **Texture note:** the guitar should feel like being wrapped in a blanket. Warm, close-mic'd, intimate, fingerpicked — not strummed. The arrangement growing should feel like the apartment warming around you.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

# IDEA E — THE TRANSFORMATION OF PLACE, NOT FACE
*Feeling: awe. She walks through one continuous space and the SPACE transforms around her every few steps — while she stays the constant. The world changes; she doesn't.*

## CONCEPT E-1 — "One Hallway, Every Season"

- **Feeling:** awe / time-passing beauty
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a single thick low side-braid, dark auburn, draped over the left shoulder, tied with a thin gold clasp at the end
- **Magic move:** she walks down ONE continuous hallway but the world outside the windows cycles through the four seasons with each step — spring blossoms, summer sun, autumn gold, winter snow — and the hallway itself shifts (wallpaper, light temperature, floor material) while she walks unchanged
- **Concept line:** "I stayed — everything else moved"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken walk-and-dolly through a transforming hallway, 7 frames
- **Loop:** the hallway returns to the spring state she started in

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | left third of screen | 8 feet from camera | front pose walking | eye-level
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **left third of screen**, approximately **8 feet from lens**. Walking toward the camera.
- **Hairstyle:** single thick low side-braid, dark auburn, over the left shoulder, thin gold clasp at the end.
- **Wardrobe:** a timeless fitted camel wool coat (mid-calf, classic cut, belt tied), over a white crew-neck tee and straight dark-wash jeans. Classic, seasonless.
- **Footwear:** clean white leather sneakers, mid-stride.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** no eyewear; small gold hoop earrings, a simple gold signet ring, warm nude glossy nails; nothing extra — she IS the constant.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front walking pose, **left third**, mid-stride, confident and unhurried.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **8 feet back**, dolly-back matching her walking speed (she stays in frame).
- **Background (powerful):** a long elegant hallway — CURRENTLY IN SPRING: soft sage-green floral wallpaper, pale wood floor, tall windows on the right showing CHERRY BLOSSOMS in full bloom outside, warm spring light flooding in, the occasional petal drifting through a cracked window. Fresh, alive, pastel.
- **Lighting:** soft warm spring light from the tall windows; the blossoms casting pink-dappled shadows on the floor.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated spring palette — sage green + cherry-blossom pink + warm pale wood + the camel coat as a grounding constant.
- **Composition:** Aira left third walking toward camera, the spring hallway receding behind her in forced perspective, blossoms visible through every window.
- **Facial Expression:** calm forward confidence — eyes ahead at the lens, a gentle half-smile, brow relaxed, chin level. She walks through changing worlds and doesn't flinch. That's the whole point.
- **Object Interaction:** mid-stride — one hand in the coat pocket, the other swinging naturally. A single blossom petal lands on her shoulder unnoticed.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 smooth dolly-back at her walking speed, maintaining 8 feet — she stays framed as the hallway recedes.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:02 unhurried forward walk, natural gait, eyes on the lens.
- **Object Action:** cherry blossoms drift through the cracked windows; spring light dapples; the petal lands on her shoulder; the wallpaper and floor maintain their spring state.
- **Physics:** petals drift with correct light-mass air-resistance; her braid sways with the walk (pendulum physics); her coat moves with real wool-weight stride-motion.
- **Object Interaction:** the petal lands on her shoulder with zero-weight contact; her natural arm-swing is precise.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 the calm look; 0:01 a gentle blink; 0:02 the half-smile holding — nothing changes on her face, which is the point.
- **Lighting Behavior:** warm spring light, dappled and soft.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — the full hallway legible.
- **Diegetic Sound:** her footsteps on pale wood (soft, rhythmic); spring birdsong through the windows; a breeze carrying petals; distant water (a stream outside); fabric swish of her stride.
- **Loop note:** spring-hallway is the master reference for the final frame.

**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`

- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter body (knees up), front walking, **center**.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 40mm, **5 feet from lens**, dollying back.
- **Background (powerful):** the hallway MID-TRANSITION from spring to SUMMER: the sage wallpaper morphing to a warm honey-gold grasscloth; the pale wood floor becoming sun-bleached oak; the windows now showing a BLAZING SUMMER landscape (golden wheat fields, tall grass, a hot blue sky, cicada-heat visible). The spring blossoms are gone — replaced by full green leaves and golden light.
- **Lighting:** BLAZING warm summer sun through the windows — strong, golden, harsh shadows, heat-haze in the light beams.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated summer — golden wheat + honey wall + hot blue sky + her camel coat now reading as part of the landscape.
- **Composition:** Aira center walking, the hallway transforming around her (the transition visible — spring at the far end behind her, summer where she IS, a seamless morph).
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged calm — the same half-smile, the same eyes on the lens. She doesn't notice or react. She IS timeless.
- **Object Interaction:** her hand reaches out and trails fingertips along the changing wallpaper — she touches summer without remarking on it.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:02–0:04 continued dolly-back, maintaining the walk-framing.
- **Subject Action:** 0:02–0:03 she walks, hand trailing the wall; 0:03–0:04 continues — unchanged.
- **Object Action:** the MORPH happens in real-time around her: wallpaper texture transitions (sage floral melting into honey grasscloth); floor lightens; the view through windows transitions (blossoms falling, green thickening, wheat appearing); light intensifies and warms; cicadas replace birdsong.
- **Physics:** the transition spreads from where she IS (she's the trigger — the world changes as she passes); wallpaper morph has texture-shift reality; light-change is gradual but clear.
- **Object Interaction:** her fingertips trail the wall and the wallpaper transitions UNDER her touch — she touches the seam between seasons.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** unchanged — the constant. A single calm blink.
- **Lighting Behavior:** spring-soft transitioning to summer-harsh — shadows shortening, intensity increasing.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus tracking the morph.
- **Diegetic Sound:** footsteps transitioning from pale-wood to sun-bleached-oak (subtly different tone); birdsong fading, cicadas rising; the heat in the sound (a warmth-hum); her steady breath.
- **Loop note:** —

- **Wardrobe:** camel coat collar in profile — reading as autumnal now.

Leaves are drifting IN through the window, landing on the hallway floor.

- **Color & Vibrance:** MAXIMUM AUTUMN — blazing orange + amber + burnt-red + dark walnut + her auburn braid as the perfect accent. Peak saturation.

**VIDEO PROMPT**

- **Physics:** leaves fall with correct mass and tumble-rate; they scatter on the floor with correct sliding physics; the frost begins at the window-edge with real ice-crystal formation.
- **Object Interaction:** leaves pass near her but she doesn't interact — she's above the seasons.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** the same. Always the same. That IS the concept.
- **Lighting Behavior:** golden-hour angle maximizing — the most dramatic, cinematic light of the whole piece.
- **Lens / Optical:** shallow — her face sharp, autumn leaves as warm soft bokeh.

### FRAME 4 — full body | center of screen | 7 feet from camera | front walking | slight low angle — WINTER
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`

- **Wardrobe:** camel coat — unchanged, but now reading perfectly AS winter-appropriate. The timelessness of the choice.
- **Footwear:** white sneakers leaving prints on the now frost-dusted floor.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** hoops with tiny frost-crystals caught, signet ring, nude nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front walking, **center**, slight low angle heroic.
- **Camera:** slight low angle, 28mm, **7 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** the hallway IN FULL WINTER: wallpaper now a deep midnight-blue with silver frost-pattern; floor a polished dark stone with a frost-sheen; windows showing a SNOW LANDSCAPE — bare black trees, deep snow, a silver-grey sky, snow falling. Snow drifts IN through the cracked windows. The hallway is cold and crystalline and BEAUTIFUL.
- **Lighting:** cold silver-blue ambient (winter light); the snow outside casting a blue-reflected glow; her warm skin the only warm-toned element.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated winter — midnight-blue + silver + white snow + black trees + her camel coat as the ONE warm constant in a cold world.
- **Composition:** Aira center, the winter hallway dramatic and crystalline around her, she the warm constant, snow entering.
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged — the half-smile, the calm eyes, the unbothered walk. Snow lands on her and she doesn't shiver. She's above seasons.
- **Object Interaction:** snowflakes land on her coat and braid — she doesn't brush them off. They're temporary. She's not.

**VIDEO PROMPT**

- **Physics:** snow drifts with correct flake-physics; frost-breath forms when she exhales (but subtly — she's warm); her footsteps on stone have correct sound; snow accumulates on her shoulders realistically.
- **Object Interaction:** snow on her coat — real contact, real tiny melt-spots.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** unchanged constant. One slow blink.
- **Lighting Behavior:** cold blue — but ahead, a faint warm glow beginning (the spring returning).
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — the winter drama legible; the first green bud visible ahead.
- **Diegetic Sound:** footsteps on cold stone (sharp); wind with snow-hiss; a deep winter silence; her frost-breath; the faintest distant birdsong beginning ahead (spring calling).
- **Loop note:** —
