### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — E-1 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** a four-season orchestral journey — one continuous musical piece that transitions through seasonal colors, like Vivaldi reimagined as a film score.
- **Tempo / key:** ~88 BPM, transitions — Spring: D major (bright), Summer: A major (blazing), Autumn: E minor (rich), Winter: C minor (crystalline), back to D major.
- **Core elements:** Spring: strings + flute; Summer: full brass + drums; Autumn: solo cello + acoustic guitar; Winter: solo piano + glass-synth; the transitions between them are seamless morphs.
- **Arc:** strings + flute (Frames 1–2, spring into summer) → brass + drums at summer peak → cello entering as autumn (Frame 3) → solo piano at winter (Frame 4) → a building return to strings + flute for spring (Frame 5–6 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the transitions must be SEAMLESS — the instruments morph into each other (flute → brass, guitar → piano) rather than cutting. One continuous evolving piece.
- **Loop:** clean 12s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT E-2 — "One Staircase, Every Era"

- **Feeling:** awe / time-travel elegance
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a sleek finger-wave bob (1920s-inspired), jet-black, sculpted and glossy, chin-length, one side pinned with an art-deco diamond clip
- **Magic move:** she descends a grand staircase and with each flight, the architecture morphs through eras — 1920s Art Deco → 1960s Mid-Century → 1980s Memphis → Modern Minimalist — while she remains the constant
- **Concept line:** "every era wanted me"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken descending-staircase track, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the staircase returns to the 1920s Art Deco opening state

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | center of screen | 8 feet from camera | three-quarter walking down | slight low angle
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **8 feet from lens**. Descending a grand staircase.
- **Hairstyle:** sleek finger-wave bob, jet-black, sculpted glossy, chin-length, art-deco diamond clip on the right side.
- **Wardrobe:** a classic black silk slip dress (bias-cut, ankle-length, thin straps), simple and timeless — reads across all eras.
- **Footwear:** black satin pointed-toe heels with a thin ankle strap — classic, era-neutral.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** the art-deco diamond clip; a long single-strand pearl rope necklace; a slim black cigarette holder (unlit, held as a prop/accessory, not smoking); deep red glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, three-quarter descending pose (one foot on a lower step, elegant), **center**.
- **Camera:** slight low angle (from the foot of the stairs looking up), 35mm, deep focus, **8 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a grand staircase in FULL ART DECO: geometric brass railings with sunburst patterns, black marble steps with gold inlay, mirrored walls with geometric etching, a massive art-deco chandelier with cascading crystal tiers, the walls in deep emerald lacquer with gold geometric trim. Gatsby opulence.
- **Lighting:** warm golden chandelier key from above; brass reflections; geometric shadow-patterns from the railings; everything glossy.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated Art Deco — deep emerald + gold + black marble + crystal white + her red nails as the sole warm-pop.
- **Composition:** Aira center descending, the geometric staircase converging behind and above her, the chandelier crowning the frame.
- **Facial Expression:** composed elegance — chin lifted slightly, eyes steady ahead and slightly down the stairs (navigating with grace), a subtle closed-lip Mona Lisa smile, brow arched with quiet authority. The "I belong in every room" face.
- **Object Interaction:** one hand glides along the brass railing (fingertips trailing, not gripping); the other holds the cigarette holder at her side with a relaxed, period-accurate pose.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 slow dolly-back descending with her (camera moves down as she descends), maintaining the low angle.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:02 she descends — slow, deliberate, elegant; each step placed.
- **Object Action:** the Art Deco environment holds; chandelier crystals sway; geometric shadows shift with her descent.
- **Physics:** her dress has correct silk-bias drape (it pools and flows with each step); the heel placement on marble is precise; the railing is cold under her trailing fingertips.
- **Object Interaction:** fingertips trail the railing with correct brass-on-skin contact; the cigarette holder stays balanced in her relaxed grip.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 composed; 0:01 the Mona Lisa smile; 0:02 a single slow blink of poise.
- **Lighting Behavior:** chandelier light shifts as she descends (the angle changes, shadows move).
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — the full Art Deco spectacle legible.
- **Diegetic Sound:** her heels on marble (sharp, rhythmic, echoing); the chandelier crystals tinkling from vibration; the brass railing singing under her fingertips; jazz piano faintly echoing (diegetic — from somewhere in this Deco world).
- **Loop note:** Art Deco state is the master reference.

---

### FRAME 2 — medium (waist up) | right of screen | 4 feet from camera | profile descending | eye-level — MID-CENTURY MORPH
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Half body (waist up) in profile, positioned **right of screen**, approximately **4 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** finger-wave bob in profile — unchanged, timeless.
- **Wardrobe:** same black silk slip — unchanged.
- **Footwear:** out of frame.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** diamond clip, pearls, cigarette holder, red nails — all unchanged.
- **Pose & Framing:** half body (waist up), descending profile, **right of screen**; the morphing staircase fills left.
- **Camera:** eye-level (beside the staircase), 50mm, **4 feet from lens**, tracking with her descent.
- **Background (powerful):** the staircase MID-MORPH to 1960s MID-CENTURY MODERN: brass geometric railings smoothing into clean teak wood; black marble becoming warm terrazzo; the emerald lacquer walls transitioning to white with bold color-block art; the chandelier simplifying into a Sputnik pendant. Clean lines replacing ornate geometry.
- **Lighting:** transitioning from warm gold to a cooler, brighter mid-century light (more even, less dramatic).
- **Color & Vibrance:** mid-century palette arriving — warm white + teak + bold primary-color art + terrazzo speckle.
- **Composition:** her profile right, the morph visible left — two eras coexisting.
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged composure — the same slight smile, the same poise. She doesn't acknowledge the change.
- **Object Interaction:** her hand now trailing teak (the railing has changed material under her fingertips).

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:02–0:04 tracking with her descent at 4 feet.
- **Subject Action:** 0:02–0:04 she descends unchanged, fingertips trailing the MORPHING railing.
- **Object Action:** the morph spreads from where she IS: brass → teak; marble → terrazzo; Deco → mid-century; chandelier simplifying; art appearing on the walls.
- **Physics:** the morph spreads smoothly; her fingertips feel the material change (a micro-adjustment in her hand angle as brass becomes wood).
- **Object Interaction:** fingers adjust to the new material — the subtle grip-change is the only acknowledgement.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** unchanged. The constant.
- **Lighting Behavior:** warmer → brighter, cleaner transition.
- **Lens / Optical:** medium depth.
- **Diegetic Sound:** heel sound transitions (marble → terrazzo — subtly different resonance); jazz piano fading, replaced by a faint bossa nova; the material change (a soft morph-sound); her steady footsteps.
- **Loop note:** —

---

### FRAME 3 — close-up (face + railing hand) | center of screen | 18 inches from camera | three-quarter pose | eye-level — 1980s MEMPHIS
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Close-up face and her hand on the railing, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **18 inches from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** finger-wave bob — unchanged, now contrasting dramatically with the Memphis chaos behind.
- **Wardrobe:** black silk strap at the shoulder.
- **Footwear:** out of frame.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** diamond clip, pearl rope, red nails on the NOW-MEMPHIS railing (bold pink and teal geometric tubing).
- **Pose & Framing:** close-up (face + hand on railing), three-quarter, **center**.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 85mm, shallow, **18 inches from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** FULL 1980s MEMPHIS DESIGN: the railing is now bold tubular steel in hot pink and teal; the walls are geometric confetti-patterns (triangles, squiggles, dots) in primary colors; the stair carpet is a bold zigzag; a neon sign glows somewhere. Maximum visual noise — which makes HER calm simplicity even more striking.
- **Lighting:** bold flat Memphis-era lighting — no moody shadows, just bright even color from multiple angles. Neon accents.
- **Color & Vibrance:** MAXIMUM CHAOS — hot pink + teal + yellow + neon + confetti-patterns — the loudest palette. Her black dress as the calm center.
- **Composition:** her calm face center, the Memphis explosion behind — the contrast IS the frame.
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged — the same composed half-smile. She is the quiet in the storm. Unbothered. Classic.
- **Object Interaction:** her red-nailed hand wraps the tubular steel railing — the red nails fitting the Memphis world as if she was always here.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:04–0:06 static intimate hold — the contrast plays.
- **Subject Action:** 0:04–0:06 she descends through the Memphis world with the same elegant pace. Unchanged.
- **Object Action:** Memphis patterns pulse slightly with energy; neon flickers; the tubular railing continues down.
- **Physics:** her grip on the tubular steel has correct cylindrical contact; the silk dress doesn't absorb the color around it — it stays BLACK, grounding.
- **Object Interaction:** hand on tube — correct cylindrical grip.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** the same. One slow blink. Absolute poise amid visual chaos.
- **Lighting Behavior:** bold, flat, bright — Memphis maximum.
- **Lens / Optical:** shallow — her face calm-sharp, the Memphis chaos soft behind.
- **Diegetic Sound:** bossa nova has become a faint synth-pop beat; her heels on carpet (muffled); the neon buzz; her steady breath.
- **Loop note:** —

---

### FRAME 4 — full body | left of screen | 7 feet from camera | front descending | eye-level — MODERN MINIMALIST
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **left of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** finger-wave bob — unchanged.
- **Wardrobe:** black slip dress — unchanged. NOW reading as the most "of the moment" thing in this minimal space.
- **Footwear:** black satin heels on the final steps — clean concrete.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** diamond clip, pearls, cigarette holder, red nails — all unchanged.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front descending, **left of screen**; the modern minimalist staircase fills right.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, **7 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** FULL MODERN MINIMALIST: the staircase is now clean white concrete with a thin black metal railing; the walls pure white; the light is one large diffused panel from above; no decoration except one single perfect flower in a vase at the landing. The anti-Memphis — pure calm.
- **Lighting:** clean, bright, single-source diffused panel — even, shadowless, gallery-like.
- **Color & Vibrance:** intentionally minimal — white + black + her skin-tone + one flower (vivid orange). The restraint IS the statement.
- **Composition:** Aira left, the minimal staircase right — empty space as design.
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged — the same half-smile. She fits here too. She fits everywhere.
- **Object Interaction:** fingertips trail the thin black metal railing — the same gesture, the latest material.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:06–0:08 dolly-back at her pace.
- **Subject Action:** 0:06–0:08 she reaches the bottom of the modern stairs and stops — the descent complete.
- **Object Action:** the minimalist space holds; the single flower sits; the panel-light is steady. And ahead — the FIRST hint of the Art Deco return (a brass glint at the edge, a geometric shadow appearing).
- **Physics:** her heels on concrete (different resonance again); the thin railing has micro-vibration from her trailing touch.
- **Object Interaction:** she pauses, releases the railing — the last touch.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** the same. Then: the TINIEST knowing brow-raise (she knows it's cycling back). The subtlest acknowledgement.
- **Lighting Behavior:** clean white — but a warm gold beginning at the frame edges (Deco returning).
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus.
- **Diegetic Sound:** heels on concrete (clean, modern); silence (the minimal world); the faint beginning of jazz piano again (Deco calling); a geometric shadow ticking into place.
- **Loop note:** —

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — E-2 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** an era-morphing soundtrack that transitions through decades — each section authentic to its era but using the SAME underlying melodic motif.
- **Tempo / key:** ~90 BPM throughout, key shifts: Deco = Bb minor (dark jazz), Mid-century = C major (bossa), Memphis = D major (synth-pop), Modern = ambient Eb (minimal).
- **Core elements — the SAME 4-bar melody played in each era's style:** Deco: jazz piano + upright bass + brushed drums; Mid-century: bossa guitar + light percussion + flute; Memphis: synth-lead + drum machine + slap bass; Modern: solo piano + silence.
- **Arc:** jazz version (Frame 1) → cross-fade to bossa (Frame 2) → cross-fade to synth-pop (Frame 3) → cross-fade to solo piano (Frame 4) → cross-fade back to jazz (Frame 5 loop close).
- **Texture note:** the melody must be RECOGNIZABLE across all four era-versions. Same notes, totally different production. That's the hook.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT E-3 — "One Bridge, Day to Night"

- **Feeling:** awe / cinematic beauty
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a voluminous blown-out curtain of platinum-silver hair, center part, waist-length, metallic sheen
- **Magic move:** she walks across one bridge and with each step the sky cycles from DAWN → GOLDEN HOUR → SUNSET → BLUE HOUR → FULL NIGHT with stars — the light transforming everything around her while she stays constant
- **Concept line:** "I walked through every hour"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken walk across a long bridge, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the night gives way to dawn again — the cycle restarts

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | right third of screen | 8 feet from camera | front walking | eye-level — DAWN
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **right third of screen**, approximately **8 feet from lens**. Walking across a bridge toward the camera.
- **Hairstyle:** voluminous blown-out platinum-silver curtain, center part, waist-length, metallic sheen catching the first dawn light.
- **Wardrobe:** a flowing silver-grey silk midi-dress with long sleeves, the fabric catching and reflecting whatever light surrounds her (it will read differently in each lighting state).
- **Footwear:** minimal silver flat strappy sandals.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** no eyewear; a thin silver chain with a crescent-moon pendant; small diamond studs; a silver cuff bracelet; soft silver-lavender glossy nails.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front walking, **right third**, mid-stride, serene.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **8 feet back**, dolly-back matching her walk.
- **Background (powerful):** an elegant pedestrian bridge (modern cable-stayed, clean lines) at DAWN — the sky a gradient of soft peach → lavender → pale blue, the horizon glowing pink-gold, the water below reflecting the pastel sky, the city skyline as a dark silhouette against the dawn. First light. Fresh and quiet.
- **Lighting:** soft dawn-light (diffused, low-angle from the horizon, peach-pink, gentle). Everything has that pre-sunrise luminosity.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated dawn — peach + lavender + soft gold + pale blue + her silver dress catching pink. Pastel but vivid.
- **Composition:** Aira right third walking, the bridge receding as perspective lines, the dawn sky dominating above.
- **Facial Expression:** serene calm — soft eyes on the lens, gentle closed-lip smile, brow relaxed, at peace with the early hour. The "this light is mine" look.
- **Object Interaction:** one hand lightly touching the cable-railing as she walks; the silver fabric catching the dawn breeze.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 dolly-back at her walking pace.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:02 she walks, unhurried, serene. Silver hair and dress catching dawn.
- **Object Action:** the dawn sky holds, then begins to BRIGHTEN — transitioning toward golden hour. The peach deepens, the gold intensifies, the horizon clarifies.
- **Physics:** her silver hair and dress move with the bridge-breeze (correct fabric/hair weight); the bridge cables vibrate imperceptibly; water below ripples.
- **Object Interaction:** fingertips trailing the cable-railing.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 serene; 0:01 soft blink; 0:02 the calm holds — unchanged.
- **Lighting Behavior:** dawn intensifying toward golden hour — the light warming, strengthening.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — the full sky/bridge scene legible.
- **Diegetic Sound:** early morning city (distant, waking); her footsteps on the bridge walkway (soft, rhythmic); the bridge cables humming in the wind; water below; birds waking; gentle breeze.
- **Loop note:** dawn state is the master reference.

---

### FRAME 2 — three-quarter body (knees up) | center of screen | 5 feet from camera | walking profile | eye-level — GOLDEN HOUR
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Three-quarter body (knees up) in profile, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **5 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** platinum-silver curtain in profile, now BLAZING in golden hour — every strand lit like molten silver-gold.
- **Wardrobe:** silver dress now reflecting warm gold — reading as liquid gold in this light.
- **Footwear:** silver sandals catching golden light.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** all silver jewelry now reading as warm gold in the light; crescent pendant catching a flare.
- **Pose & Framing:** three-quarter body, walking profile, **center**; the golden-hour bridge behind.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 50mm, **5 feet from lens**, traveling.
- **Background (powerful):** the bridge at GOLDEN HOUR — the sky blazing warm gold and amber, the water below liquid gold, the city skyline glowing, long shadows stretching, everything warm and luminous. The most beautiful light.
- **Lighting:** full golden-hour blaze — warm, directional, dramatic shadows, her silver becoming gold.
- **Color & Vibrance:** MAXIMUM GOLDEN — warm amber + liquid gold + her silver-reading-as-gold + the saturated sky. Peak warmth.
- **Composition:** her gold-lit profile center, the golden world behind — she IS the light.
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged serene — the same gentle smile in profile. Unbothered by beauty.
- **Object Interaction:** her silver cuff catches and throws a golden flare.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:02–0:04 traveling alongside her.
- **Subject Action:** 0:02–0:04 walking unchanged, the golden light painting her.
- **Object Action:** the sky transitions golden hour → the first hints of SUNSET (deeper oranges, a streak of magenta appearing at the horizon).
- **Physics:** golden-hour shadows lengthen in real time; her hair catches increasingly dramatic side-light; the bridge cables throw long geometric shadows.
- **Object Interaction:** the cuff flare moves with her arm-swing.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** unchanged. One slow blink catching the golden light on her lashes.
- **Lighting Behavior:** golden intensifying → first sunset oranges entering.
- **Lens / Optical:** the golden light creates a natural warmth-filter.
- **Diegetic Sound:** footsteps; the bridge humming; birds (golden-hour chorus); distant city; the breeze now warmer.
- **Loop note:** —

### FRAME 3 — close-up (face) | left of screen | 2 feet from camera | front pose | slight low angle — SUNSET
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Close-up face and shoulders, positioned **left of screen**, approximately **2 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** platinum hair now catching deep orange and magenta sunset — reading as rose-gold.
- **Wardrobe:** silver dress collar reflecting sunset fire.
- **Footwear:** out of frame.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** diamond studs catching orange fire; crescent pendant lit amber.
- **Pose & Framing:** close-up, front, **left of screen**, the SUNSET blazing right.
- **Camera:** slight low angle, 85mm, shallow, **2 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** a FULL DRAMATIC SUNSET behind and beside her — the sky layered with orange, magenta, purple, gold; the sun a blazing disc at the horizon visible past the bridge cables. Cinematic peak.
- **Lighting:** sunset fire — intense warm-directional from the setting sun; her face half-lit amber, half in cool shadow. Maximum drama.
- **Color & Vibrance:** SUNSET MAXIMUM — orange + magenta + purple + gold + her silver-as-rose-gold.
- **Composition:** her face left, the blazing sunset filling right — she shares the frame with the spectacle.
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged gentle calm — the sun is setting spectacularly and she wears the same soft smile. Not awed — at home. As if this happens for her every day. One slow blink.
- **Object Interaction:** the sun-warmth is visible on her skin — a golden flush; her hair lifts slightly in the evening thermal.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:04–0:06 static hold — the sunset plays.
- **Subject Action:** 0:04–0:06 she walks through, face catching the fire.
- **Object Action:** the sun SETS in real time — descending, the sky deepening, the blues beginning to appear. Transitioning toward blue hour.
- **Physics:** the sun descends with correct speed; colors shift on her face in real time; thermal-lift in her hair.
- **Object Interaction:** the sunset paints her — it's the world interacting with her.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** unchanged. The constant. Beautiful.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the most dramatic shift — warm sunset draining, cool blue-hour creeping from above.
- **Lens / Optical:** shallow — her face sharp, sunset melting to fire-bokeh.
- **Diegetic Sound:** the sunset wind; distant murmuration of starlings; bridge humming deeper (cooler air); her footsteps; the last birdsong fading.
- **Loop note:** —

### FRAME 4 — full body | center of screen | 7 feet from camera | front walking | eye-level — FULL NIGHT
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** platinum-silver hair now glowing MOONLIT — the silver reading as pure silver again in the blue-black night, luminous.
- **Wardrobe:** silver dress now reflecting the city lights and stars — reading as a starfield itself, mercury-liquid.
- **Footwear:** silver sandals catching bridge-lamp light.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** diamond studs as stars; crescent pendant = the moon (perfect symbolism); silver cuff reflecting city lights.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, front walking, **center**, the night sky above.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **7 feet from lens**.
- **Background (powerful):** the bridge at FULL NIGHT — the sky deep indigo-black FILLED with visible stars and the Milky Way (the city-light reduced for visibility); the bridge now lit by elegant warm lamp-posts along its length; the city skyline glowing with thousands of warm windows; the water below reflecting both stars and city lights — a mirror of everything.
- **Lighting:** cool blue-silver moonlight ambient + warm bridge-lamp practicals = dual-temperature beauty.
- **Color & Vibrance:** saturated night — deep indigo + star-white + warm city-amber + her silver as the connector between warm and cool.
- **Composition:** Aira center walking under the stars, bridge-lamps as warm sentinels, the Milky Way arcing above her — she walks beneath the universe.
- **Facial Expression:** unchanged. The same serene half-smile. Stars above, city below, she walks between them.
- **Object Interaction:** bridge-lamp light washes over her as she passes each one — a rhythmic warm/cool alternation.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:06–0:08 dolly-back at her pace under the stars.
- **Subject Action:** 0:06–0:08 she walks the night bridge unchanged. The constant.
- **Object Action:** stars visible; bridge-lamps pass; the city glows; and ahead — the horizon begins to lighten (the first hint of dawn returning).
- **Physics:** her silver dress and hair catch each bridge-lamp as she passes (a rhythmic lighting pulse); the stars hold correct constellation patterns; city reflections ripple on the water.
- **Object Interaction:** the rhythmic lamp-wash as she passes each post.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** unchanged — one slow blink. Peace.
- **Lighting Behavior:** the alternating warm lamp / cool moonlight rhythm as she walks.
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — stars, bridge, city, all legible.
- **Diegetic Sound:** night city (distant, quieter); her footsteps (echoing more in the night air); the bridge humming (a deeper tone at night); the water; a single distant ship-horn; crickets from the riverbank.
- **Loop note:** —

---

- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — matched.
- **Diegetic Sound:** dawn city; footsteps; cables; water; birds — looping cleanly.
- **Loop note:** **LOOP POINT** — positions, light, time-of-day state, and expression match Frame 1 exactly.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — E-3 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** a cinematic time-lapse score — one continuous build that transitions through time-of-day moods, like a Hans Zimmer slow-burn.
- **Tempo / key:** builds — 70 BPM → 90 BPM → 100 BPM → back to 70. Key: starts F major (dawn), peaks at Bb major (sunset), deepens to D minor (night), returns to F major (dawn).
- **Core elements:** dawn: solo piano + soft strings; golden hour: full strings swelling; sunset: strings + brass + a building percussive pulse; night: stripped to solo cello + ambient synth-pad + distant piano; dawn return: solo piano.
- **Arc:** gentle piano (Frame 1 dawn) → strings building (Frame 2 golden hour) → full orchestral peak at sunset (Frame 3) → stripped intimate cello at night (Frame 4) → return to solo piano (Frame 5 dawn loop).
- **Texture note:** the build from dawn to sunset should feel INEVITABLE — like watching a sunrise from space, accelerated. The night drop should feel like a release, not a collapse.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT E-4 — "One Street, Every Weather"

- **Feeling:** awe / primal satisfaction
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** long box braids gathered into a high thick ponytail, jet-black with thin gold thread woven through select braids, reaching mid-back
- **Magic move:** she walks down one city street and with each block the WEATHER transforms — bright sunshine → gentle fog → pouring rain → thick snow → back to sunshine — while she walks unbothered and unchanged, no umbrella, no coat-change
- **Concept line:** "I don't check the forecast"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken walk down a city street with transforming weather, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the sunshine returns to the opening state

---

- **Wardrobe:** a crisp white oversized linen blazer over a black fitted crop-top, high-waist black wide-leg trousers — sharp and weather-inappropriate (she wears it through EVERYTHING).
- **Footwear:** black patent pointed-toe loafers, glossy.
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** slim gold rectangular sunglasses; multiple thin gold chains layered at the neck; gold hoop earrings (medium); a gold watch; black glossy almond nails.

- **Object Interaction:** her braided ponytail swings with the stride; the gold chains bounce slightly with each step.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — E-4 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** a cool, unflinching walk-track with weather-texture shifts — the musical equivalent of not checking the forecast.
- **Tempo / key:** ~100 BPM throughout (unwavering, like her pace), C# minor, confident and dark-luxe.
- **Core elements:** a driving bass-line (constant, never changes — like her); a crisp snare on the 2-and-4 (her footstep-beat); over this constant rhythm, the TEXTURE changes with each weather: sunshine = clean, dry, bright synths; fog = muffled, reverbed, filtered; rain = distorted, compressed, heavy; snow = stripped, quiet, space; sunshine return = clean again.
- **Arc:** the bass and snare NEVER change. Only the texture on top shifts. The rhythm is her. The texture is the weather. The point: she stays the same, everything else moves around her.
- **Texture note:** the bass and snare MUST be identical in every section — the absolute constant, like her walk. Only the layered textures shift. This IS the concept musically.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.

## CONCEPT E-5 — "One Garden, From Seed to Ancient Tree"

- **Feeling:** awe / life / time compressed
- **Hairstyle (this concept):** a sleek centre-part bun with two long face-framing tendrils, dark brown with a single bold white streak at the front (like Cruella, but elegant)
- **Magic move:** she walks through a garden and with each step, TIME accelerates around her — a seed sprouts, becomes a sapling, grows into a young tree, ages into a massive ancient oak with moss and roots, then cycles to autumn/decay/new seed — while she stays young, unchanged, walking through centuries in seconds
- **Concept line:** "time moved — I didn't"
- **Continuous shot:** one unbroken walk through a garden that ages around her, 6 frames
- **Loop:** the ancient tree drops a seed — the garden resets to the beginning, ready to grow again

---

### FRAME 1 — full body | center of screen | 7 feet from camera | three-quarter walking | eye-level — SEED/BARE EARTH
**IMAGE PROMPT**
- **Subject:** `Aira, [placeholder]`
- **Anti-flip:** Do not mirror, flip, or invert the subject. Maintain consistent left-right orientation throughout.
- **Subject Framing:** Full body head-to-feet, positioned **center of screen**, approximately **7 feet from lens**.
- **Hairstyle:** sleek centre-part bun with two long face-framing tendrils, dark brown with bold white streak at the front.
- **Wardrobe:** a timeless fitted dark-green wool dress (midi, long-sleeve, mock-neck), simple, elegant — reading as "beyond time."
- **Footwear:** bare feet on earth (grounding, timeless, connected).
- **Eyewear / Jewelry / Nails / Accessories:** no eyewear; a thin vine-shaped gold ring (botanical motif); small green-stone stud earrings (emerald); bare, natural nails; a single seed held between her thumb and forefinger.
- **Pose & Framing:** full body, three-quarter walking, **center**, pausing to place the seed in the ground.
- **Camera:** eye-level, 35mm, deep focus, **7 feet back**.
- **Background (powerful):** a garden space that is currently BARE EARTH — rich dark soil, a single cleared plot surrounded by a stone garden wall, a soft morning mist, and distant established trees beyond the wall. The potential of emptiness. Dawn light. Expectation.
- **Lighting:** soft misty dawn — diffused, cool, fresh, dewy; low-angle first light.
- **Color & Vibrance:** muted potential — dark rich earth + her dark-green dress + the mist + dawn — grounded, expecting.
- **Composition:** Aira center crouching to plant, the bare earth surrounding, the stone wall as boundary, distant trees as promise.
- **Facial Expression:** focused tenderness — eyes on the seed, brow soft with intention, a gentle closed-lip smile of hope, the face of someone planting something they know will outlive them.
- **Object Interaction:** she crouches (three-quarter body still visible) and presses the seed INTO the earth with her fingertip — the exact moment of planting. Her fingertip makes contact with the soil; the seed transfers from her to the ground.

**VIDEO PROMPT**
- **Camera Movement:** 0:00–0:02 static hold at 7 feet — the planting moment.
- **Subject Action:** 0:00–0:01 she crouches, places the seed; 0:01–0:02 stands, steps back — and the seed IMMEDIATELY begins to sprout.
- **Object Action:** the seed hits earth and a GREEN SHOOT emerges — fast, alive, pushing through the soil with time-lapse speed. Growing visibly as she watches.
- **Physics:** the shoot emerges with correct plant-growth physics (spiraling, unfurling, phototropic) but at massively accelerated speed; soil crumbles around it; her dress shifts as she stands.
- **Object Interaction:** the finger-to-soil contact is precise — the seed pressed in with correct depth; the soil gives under her fingertip.
- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:00 focused planting; 0:01 she stands — eyes on the shoot, surprise-delight, brow up; 0:02 the gentle smile deepens.
- **Lighting Behavior:** dawn light beginning to intensify (time accelerating).
- **Lens / Optical:** deep focus — the shoot and her equally sharp.
- **Diegetic Sound:** morning silence; the soil taking the seed (a soft earth-sound); then: the shoot emerging (a quiet CRACKLE of growth — like ice in reverse); her inhale of delight; birds starting.
- **Loop note:** bare earth + dawn is the master reference.

- **Facial Expression Beats:** 0:04 the calm; 0:05 the look up (one brow lifts — a tiny acknowledgement of scale); 0:06 the return to the calm smile.
- **Lighting Behavior:** dappled light shifting as canopy sways — her face moving through spots of gold and shade.
- **Lens / Optical:** the wide angle makes the tree immense; she stays sharp.

### FRAME 4 — close-up (her hand on bark + falling seed) | center of screen | 12 inches from camera | macro
**IMAGE PROMPT**

- **Composition:** her hand center, the acorn landing beside it — the SEED RETURNING. The cycle completing.

- **Object Interaction:** the acorn lands beside her thumb with the tiniest "tap" — the next generation. She doesn't pick it up. It doesn't need her this time. It knows what to do.

- **Object Action:** the acorn lands; the ancient tree begins to SHED — leaves falling, the bark greying, autumn arriving at time-lapse speed. The cycle turning toward winter/decay/renewal.

- **Object Interaction:** the acorn lands with correct tiny-mass contact on the moss.

### ☆ EXTERNAL AUDIO BLOCK — E-5 (background music / sound bed)
- **Genre / vibe:** organic cinematic growth-score — nature + time + patience. The musical equivalent of watching a tree grow in time-lapse.
- **Tempo / key:** accelerating — starts ~60 BPM (planting, patient) → builds to ~110 BPM (full growth, the ancient tree peak) → decelerates back to 60 BPM (the cycle close).
- **Core elements:** solo fingerpicked acoustic guitar (the "planting" theme — patient, simple); building layers of organic instruments — flute for the sapling, full strings for the mature tree, a deep cello drone for the ancient tree, a single piano note for the falling seed; returns to solo guitar.
- **Arc:** solo guitar (Frame 1 — the seed) → guitar + flute growing (Frame 2 — the young tree) → FULL STRINGS + CELLO at the ancient tree (Frame 3 — the peak, overwhelming organic beauty) → single piano note at the acorn-fall (Frame 4 — time turning) → solo guitar return (Frame 5 — the loop, patient again).
- **Texture note:** the build must feel ORGANIC — not electronic, not processed. Like the music itself is growing from a seed. Real instruments layering like branches.
- **Loop:** clean 10s loop matching the visual loop point.
